6:248:7299:14:0:72:75:82:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
7:249:7300:0:13:275:323:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Abstract 
7:250:7308:13:14:72:75:745:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
7:251:7308:14:17:76:525:731:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:This paper discusses the magnitude of Nonperforming Loans (NPL) in the banking sector of 
7:252:7397:17:16:76:526:714:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Bangladesh   since   the   adaptation   of   prudential   norms   in   the   loan   classification   and 
7:253:7502:16:17:76:526:698:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:provisioning  system  in  1990.  Smooth  and  efficient  flow  of  saving-investment  process  is  a 
7:254:7603:17:17:76:525:681:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:prerequisite  for  the  economic  development  of  a  country.  Bangladesh,  being  a  developed 
7:255:7700:17:16:76:526:664:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:country and with an underdeveloped capital market, mainly depends on the intermediary role 
7:256:7790:16:17:76:525:648:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of  commercial  banks  for  mobilizing  internal  saving  and  providing  capital  to  the  investor. 
7:257:7892:17:16:76:525:631:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Thus,  it  matters  greatly  how  well  our  financial  sector  is  functioning.  The  process  of 
7:258:7991:16:17:76:526:615:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:economic  development  of  Bangladesh  has  been  seriously  constrained  by  the  continuing 
7:259:8085:17:16:76:525:598:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:crisis  of  the  accumulation  of  classified  loans.  As  Loan  is  the  prime  asset  of  a  bank,  it  is 
7:260:8194:16:17:76:525:582:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:essential  to  know  the  asset  quality  of  a  bank,  regulation  helps  to  determine  the  financial 
7:261:8299:17:16:76:526:565:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:health  and  efficiency  of  the  banking  sector.  Besides,  a  proper  loan  classification  and 
7:262:8398:16:17:76:525:549:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:provisioning system ensures credibility of the financial system that in turn restores trust and 
7:263:8494:17:17:76:525:532:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:confidence  in  the  mind  of  depositors.  Loan  classification  and  provisioning  system  is  also 
7:264:8596:17:16:76:526:515:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:essential  for  regularizing  follow-up,  monitoring  activities  and  improving  the  recovery 
7:265:8692:16:17:76:525:499:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:position. However, the criteria for classifying and provisioning loan portfolios depend on the 
7:266:8787:17:16:76:267:482:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:prudential policies of the central bank.  
7:267:8828:16:17:76:94:466:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:      
7:268:8833:17:16:76:526:449:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:There are several reasons of classified  loans  in our banking sector such as  flow problem of 
7:269:8928:16:17:76:525:433:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:bad  loans,  dissatisfactory  performance  of  the  courts,  having  no  concrete  NPL  management 
7:270:9027:17:17:76:525:416:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:strategy equipped with both preventive and resolution measures, having no measurement of 
7:271:9116:17:16:76:526:399:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the meaningful application of the CRG device in the credit environment etc. For this, there is 
7:272:9211:16:17:76:525:383:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:huge amount of classified  loans  in our banking  sector. The Bangladesh  Bank  has given the 
7:273:9305:17:16:76:525:366:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:guidelines  regarding  the  provisioning  system  against  classified  loans  through  the  BCD  and 
7:274:9406:16:17:76:526:350:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:BRPD  circulation.    Due  to  increasing  default  risks  of  loans,  the  provisioning  system  has 
7:275:9508:17:16:76:525:333:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:been revised several times. For protecting the depositor‟s interest and keeping the bank‟s 
7:276:9599:16:17:76:525:317:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:financial  condition  solvent  huge  amount  of  provisions  are  kept  against  the  classified  loans. 
7:277:9704:17:17:76:526:300:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:For the causes of classified  loans, provision of the banking  sector is  increasing. As a result 
7:278:9802:17:16:76:525:283:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the profit of the banks is coming down. Besides government also deprive from current year 
7:279:9892:16:17:76:274:267:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:taxes due to higher rate of provisioning.  
7:280:9934:17:16:76:79:250:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
7:281:9934:16:17:76:526:234:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:So it is needed to maintain a standard asset quality and so need to follow related prudential 
7:282:10027:17:16:76:525:217:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:regulation.  Besides,  maintenance  of  an  ethical  standard  in  the  banking  profession  from  all 
7:283:10130:16:17:76:525:201:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:concerns  can  be  viewed  as  an  important  means  for  making  the  credit  environment  credible 
7:284:10231:17:16:76:526:184:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:and  vibrant. We  have had a two-decade long  experience  in dealing with the NPLs problem 
7:285:10322:16:17:76:525:168:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:and  much  is known  about the causes and remedies of the problem. So,  it  is  very  important 
7:286:10418:17:17:76:525:151:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:for  the  lenders,  borrowers  and  policy  makers  to  learn  from  the  past  experience  and  act 
7:287:10519:17:16:76:521:134:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:accordingly. It is optimistic that at present the trend of classified loans has begun to decline. 
7:288:10616:16:17:76:79:118:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
7:289:10616:17:16:76:79:101:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
7:290:10616:16:0:72:75:85:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
8:291:10617:0:14:245:319:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Chapter- One 
8:292:10628:14:26:251:314:744:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Introduction 
8:293:10640:26:21:72:75:718:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
8:294:10640:21:14:72:243:697:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:1.1 Background of the Study: 
8:295:10667:14:13:72:75:683:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
8:296:10667:13:17:72:526:670:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Most of the business is done by banks with the funds which are collected from the public by 
8:297:10759:17:17:72:526:653:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:way of deposits. A non-performing asset in the banking sector may be termed as an asset not 
8:298:10851:17:16:72:526:636:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:contributing to the  income of the  bank. In other words, it  is a zero  yield  asset when applied 
8:299:10950:16:17:72:526:620:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:particularly  to  loan  and  advances.  The  actual  concept  of  NPA  is  that  it  is  an  asset  which 
8:300:11056:17:16:72:525:603:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:ceases to yield income for the bank and that any income accrued from such asset shall not be 
8:301:11149:16:17:72:526:587:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:treated as income until  it  is actually realized.  Classification of an asset as NPA  should  be  a 
8:302:11250:17:16:72:526:570:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:based  on  record  of  recovery.  Therefore,  an  asset  is  to  be  classified  as  NPA  when  there  is  a 
8:303:11359:16:17:72:526:554:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:threat  of  loss  for  the  recoverability  is  in  doubt.  In  spite  of  wide  ranging  reform  measures 
8:304:11466:17:17:72:526:537:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:initiated in the banking sector, the problem of non-performing assets assumed a central place 
8:305:11560:17:16:72:250:520:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:in issues relating to banking sector.   
8:306:11599:16:14:72:77:504:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:  
8:307:11599:14:17:72:525:490:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Lending  function of a  bank  needs to add value to the  bank. The  lending  function comprises 
8:308:11695:17:16:72:526:473:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:origination, funding, monitoring and servicing of loan. Loans are deemed as assets of a bank. 
8:309:11789:16:17:72:526:457:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:To  maintain  asset  to  a  standard  quality  various  prudential  regulation  from  various  angle, 
8:310:11891:17:16:72:526:440:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:issued by central bank such as, loan classification criteria, provisioning requirement, income 
8:311:11986:16:17:72:502:424:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:recognition, write-off policy, risk diversification, directed lending, debt restructuring etc. 
8:312:12080:17:16:72:75:407:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
8:313:12080:16:17:72:526:391:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:In  the  absence  of  strong  capital  market,  Bangladesh  depends  heavily  on  the  banking  sector 
8:314:12183:17:17:72:526:374:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:for a smooth financial  intermediation. However,  for many  years  Bangladeshi  banking  sector 
8:315:12279:17:16:72:526:357:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:has been burdened with the crisis of accumulation of huge non-performing loans. All types of 
8:316:12372:16:17:72:526:341:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:domestic banks i.e. NCBs, PCBs and DFIs are facing the daunting amount of non-performing 
8:317:12461:17:16:72:526:324:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:loan.  Since  1980s,  the  central  banks  of  the  developing  countries,  following  the  practices  of 
8:318:12567:16:17:72:526:308:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:the developed countries, have adopted the “prudential norms for asset classification”, with a 
8:319:12661:17:16:72:525:291:12:Times New Roman:12:g_d0_f9:view to ensuring “transparency” and “quality” of the loan portfolios of the banks. It is a part 
8:320:12756:16:17:72:292:275:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of Financial Sector Reform Program (FSRP). 
8:321:12798:17:14:72:75:258:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
8:322:12798:14:16:72:526:244:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Bangladesh,  too,  has  started  adopting  a  number  of  financial  sector  reform  measures  since 
8:323:12899:16:17:72:529:228:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:1990  as  a  part  of  its  overall  economic  stabilization  and  structural  adjustment  program.  
8:324:13000:17:16:72:526:211:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Though    privatization    (allowing    new    private    commercial    banks    to    operate)    and 
8:325:13103:16:17:72:526:195:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:denationalization  (selling  out  government  banks  to  private  entrepreneurs)  of  the  financial 
8:326:13204:17:16:72:525:178:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:institutions (as well as other real sector enterprises) started well before (in 1983) the adoption 
8:327:13303:16:17:72:388:162:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of stabilization and structural adjustment program by Bangladesh 
8:328:13367:17:17:72:526:145:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Government.  However,  even  if  we  consider  1990  as  take-off  year  in  regard  to  financial 
8:329:13466:17:16:72:525:128:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:reforms,  we  have  by  this  time  passed  22  years  of reforms.  The  main  features  of  Financial 
8:330:13569:16:17:72:526:112:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Sector  Reforms  Program  (FSRP)  in  the  context  of  banking  sector  of  Bangladesh  are: 
8:331:13663:17:16:72:526:95:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:liberalization of  interest rate policy, abolition of refinance and  introduction of rediscounting 
8:332:13762:16:0:72:525:79:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:scheme, introduction of new system of loan classification and provisioning, capital adequacy 
9:333:13855:0:16:72:526:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:requirement, strengthening of Central Bank, improvement in the operation of NCBs (recently 
9:334:13946:16:17:72:526:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:changed  in  Ltd  company),  computerization  of  banks,  development  of  human  resources, 
9:335:14039:17:16:72:526:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:reforms  in  the  legal  environment,  reforms  in  foreign  exchange  regime  and  development  of 
9:336:14139:16:17:72:146:709:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:capital market. 
9:337:14154:17:16:72:75:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
9:338:14154:16:17:72:526:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:After  the  introduction  of  explicit  loan  classification  system  in  1989,  loan  classification 
9:339:14256:17:17:72:526:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:system  has  undergone  a  number  of  changes  from  time  to  time.  The  present  classification 
9:340:14355:17:16:72:526:642:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:system  is  a  little  bit  relaxed  compared  to  the  international  norms  of  classifying  the  loan. 
9:341:14461:16:17:72:523:626:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Almost  a  quarter  of  the  total  loans  of  the  banking  sector  are  now  classified  or  non-
9:342:14560:17:16:72:526:609:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:performing.  According  to  latest  BRPD  (Banking  Regulation  and  Policy  Department, 2012) 
9:343:14654:16:17:72:526:593:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:circular  of  Bangladesh  Bank  the  latest  figure  indicated  that  the  6.59  %  of  total  loan  is 
9:344:14758:17:16:72:526:576:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:classified. Although, the ratio was as 26.09% since in 1990 and high as 41.1% in 1999 and it 
9:345:14851:16:17:72:322:560:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:came down gradually to the present level of 6.59%. 
9:346:14901:17:17:72:75:543:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
9:347:14901:17:16:72:526:526:12:Times New Roman:12:g_d0_f9:It  is  obvious  that  non-performing loan (NPLs) reduce banks‟ profitability, as banks cannot 
9:348:14996:16:17:72:526:510:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:appropriate  interest  income  from  their  classified  loans.  NPLs  reduce  loan-able  funds  by 
9:349:15095:17:16:72:526:493:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:stopping recycling. Banks  need to set aside a portion of their  income as  loan  loss reserve to 
9:350:15193:16:17:72:526:477:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:make up bad debt. A bank with a high percentage of NPLs suffers from erosion of the capital. 
9:351:15286:17:16:72:526:460:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:All those adverse impact of NPLs on banks‟ financial health such as low profitability and low 
9:352:15380:16:17:72:526:444:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:capital base are clearly reflected in Bangladesh banking sector. The question arises as to why 
9:353:15475:17:16:72:526:427:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:we  are  unable  to  solve  this  problem  for  such  a  long  time?  A  number  of  studies  have  been 
9:354:15580:16:17:72:526:411:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:undertaken  to  deal  with  the  problem  and  to  address  this  „default  culture‟  phenomenon. 
9:355:15678:17:17:72:526:394:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Emergence  and  accumulation  of  high  scale  of  non-performing  loans  after  independence 
9:356:15772:17:16:72:526:377:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:starting  from  the  nationalization  of  banks  has  been  well  discussed  by  a  number  of  authors 
9:357:15876:16:17:72:263:361:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(Islam et al., 1999; Moral et al., 2000).  
9:358:15918:17:13:72:75:344:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
9:359:15918:13:17:72:526:331:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Several  attempts  have  been  made  to  explain  the  non-performing  loans  problem  with  some 
9:360:16016:17:17:72:525:314:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:theories  relating  to  political  economy  backed  by  empirical  findings.    Islam  et  al.,  (1999)  in 
9:361:16124:17:16:72:526:297:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:their study on bank loan default offered the idea of „comprador government‟ and „comprador 
9:362:16215:16:17:72:526:281:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:bourgeoisie‟ developed  by Paul Baran as an explanation of the  behavior of  Bangladeshi 
9:363:16304:17:16:72:526:264:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:capitalists class where trading as opposed to manufacturing becomes the main business of the 
9:364:16397:16:17:72:526:248:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:capitalists  and  they  act  as  importers,  indentors,  sales  agents,  suppliers,  etc.  The  same  study 
9:365:16505:17:16:72:526:231:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:also   made   an  effort  to  explain  the  process  of  transfer  of  economic   surplus  through 
9:366:16604:16:17:72:526:215:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:international trade based on Emmanuel‟s theory of „unequal exchange‟ which complements 
9:367:16691:17:17:72:523:198:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:Baran‟s explanation. Ahmad (1997) used three theoretical paradigms in his quest for a socio-
9:368:16783:17:16:72:525:181:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:political  explanation  of  the  bank  loan  default  problem  of  Bangladesh,  the  rational  actor 
9:369:16884:16:17:72:526:165:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:theory, the pluralist instrumentalist theory and the organizational bargaining theory. Based on 
9:370:16980:17:16:72:526:148:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:an  investigation  he  mentioned  some  important  factors  as  causes  of  loan  default  which 
9:371:17077:16:17:72:526:132:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:includes  lack  of  willingness  to  pay  coupled  with  diversion  of  fund,  willful  negligence  and 
9:372:17181:17:16:72:526:115:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:belief  that  waiver  may  be  available  in  the  future,  operational  problems,  inability  to  utilize 
9:373:17288:16:17:72:526:99:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:production  capacity,  power  failure,  improper  credit  appraisal,  natural  calamity,  and  unfair 
9:374:17390:17:0:72:526:82:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:taxation.  Non-professional  handling  of  assets  both  by  the  NCBs  and  the  private  sector  bank 
10:375:17495:0:16:72:526:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:was reported as the main reasons for the accumulation of loan default problem in Bangladesh 
10:376:17587:16:17:72:526:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(Alam  and  Jahan,  1999).  It  included  the  Government  directed  credit  for  the  loss  making 
10:377:17687:17:16:72:526:725:12:Times New Roman:12:g_d0_f9:public sector enterprises and the private sector banks‟  lending to insiders and connected 
10:378:17778:16:17:72:526:709:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:parties.  Prof.  Rehman  Sobhan  (1991)  in  his  study  on  debt  default  problem  examined  the 
10:379:17877:17:16:72:500:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:nature and problems relating to poor repayment status of the two DFIs-BSB and BSRS.   
10:380:17961:16:17:72:75:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
10:381:17961:17:17:72:526:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Government of Bangladesh  has taken some  initiative such as tightening up of the regulatory 
10:382:18054:17:16:72:526:642:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:measures  to  enable  banks  to  recover  loans  from  the  defaulters.  They  have  taken  some 
10:383:18151:16:17:72:526:626:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:measures  on  recovery  of  defaulted  loan  such  as  Artha  Rin  Adalat  Ain  (Money  Loan  Court 
10:384:18251:17:16:72:526:609:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Act 2003) was enacted in 2003 with a view to improving the legal framework for recovery of 
10:385:18342:16:17:72:526:593:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:overdue  loans  and  advances  by  the  banks  and  financial  institutions.  In  recognition  of  the 
10:386:18445:17:16:72:526:576:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:importance  of  an  effective  risk  management  system,  BB  has  issued  guidelines  on  managing 
10:387:18545:16:17:72:526:560:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:core  risks  in  banking  in  October  2003.  The  five  core  risks  are  Credit  Risks,  Asset  and 
10:388:18647:17:17:72:526:543:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Liability Risks, Foreign Exchange Risks, Internal Control and Compliance Risks and Money 
10:389:18736:17:16:72:526:526:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Laundering  Risks.  Now  banks  are  not  allowed  to  approve  large  loans  in  favor  of  any 
10:390:18833:16:17:72:526:510:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:individual or group of borrowers in excess of 50  percent of their total capital. Loans, which 
10:391:18928:17:16:72:526:493:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:have been classified as bad/loss for 5 years or more against which full provision s have been 
10:392:19022:16:17:72:361:477:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:kept are to be written off by the banks to clean their books.  
10:393:19084:17:16:72:75:460:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
10:394:19084:16:17:72:526:444:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Despite  massive  injection  of  loans  to  the  national  economy,  the  contribution  of  financial 
10:395:19186:17:16:72:526:427:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:sector  to  the  Gross  Domestic  Product  (GDP)  remained  at  dismal  level.  This  laden  loan 
10:396:19284:16:17:72:526:411:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:contribution to GDP by the unhealthy and inefficient financial situation. Political connections 
10:397:19380:17:17:72:526:394:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:have played a key role in sanctioning a loan. In such connection, we should realize that what 
10:398:19474:17:16:72:526:377:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:will happen of the confidence of depositors and productive sectors borrower in the domestic 
10:399:19566:16:17:72:526:361:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:financial  system?  What will  happen if the defaulters are  not brought to book and  soundness 
10:400:19662:17:16:72:270:344:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of financial institutions are not ensured?  
10:401:19705:16:17:72:75:328:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
10:402:19705:17:16:72:215:311:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:1.2 Objectives of the Study: 
10:403:19733:16:18:72:430:295:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Managements of NPA would have the following three specific objectives: 
10:404:19803:18:16:94:518:277:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Improving the quality of NPA to a performing status so that income on such assets is 
10:405:19889:16:18:94:153:261:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:recognized. 
10:406:19900:18:17:94:508:243:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman:  Upgrading the status of the assets so as to reduce the provisioning requirements.  . 
10:407:19985:17:17:94:526:226:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To  analyze  legal  aspect  to  recover  loans  from  the  defaulters  and  the  causes  and 
10:408:20079:17:16:94:264:209:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:remedies of non-performing loans.

11:443:22166:17:17:72:526:326:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:seventh chapter contains the  findings, challenges  and concluding remarks on  nonperforming

12:464:22331:21:14:72:458:667:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:22..11  Management of NPL: Meaning, Causes, Objectives and Framework  
12:465:22397:14:16:72:75:653:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:  
12:466:22397:16:16:72:201:637:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:2.1.1 Meaning of NPA: 
12:467:22417:16:17:72:526:621:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:The  bank  being  financial  intermediaries  are  in  the  business  of  accepting  deposits  for  the 
12:468:22520:17:16:72:526:604:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:purpose  of  lending  and  to  augment  their  resources  at  times  they  borrow  money  from  other 
12:469:22622:16:17:72:526:588:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:sources  and  meet  the  ever  increasing  borrowing  requirements  of  their  customers.  However, 
12:470:22722:17:16:72:526:571:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:most of the business is done by banks with the funds which are collected from the public by 
12:471:22814:16:17:72:525:555:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:way of deposits. They are, therefore, answerable to the public at large, who are keeping their 
12:472:22908:17:17:72:526:538:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:funds  with  the  banks  by  reposing  trust  in  the  ability  of  banks  that  they  will  not  put  the 
12:473:23015:17:16:72:222:521:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:depositors interest to jeopardy. 
12:474:23047:16:17:72:75:505:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
12:475:23047:17:16:72:526:488:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: A non-performing asset  in the banking sector may  be termed as an asset not contributing to 
12:476:23140:16:17:72:526:472:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the  income  of  the  bank.  In  other  words,  it  is  a  zero  yield  asset  when  applied  particularly  to 
12:477:23251:17:16:72:526:455:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:loan  and  advances.  The  actual  concept  of  NPA  is  that  it  is  an  asset  which  ceases  to  yield 
12:478:23358:16:17:72:526:439:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:income  for  the  bank  and  that  any income  accrued  from  such  asset  shall  not  be  treated  as 
12:479:23461:17:17:72:526:422:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:income  until  it  is  actually  realized.    Classification  of  an  asset  as  NPA  should  be  a  based  on 
12:480:23572:17:16:72:526:405:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:record  of  recovery.  Therefore,  an  asset  is  to  be  classified  as  NPA  when  there  is  a  threat  of 
12:481:23682:16:17:72:525:389:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:loss  for  the  recoverability  is  in  doubt.  In  spite  of  wide  ranging  reform  measures  initiated  in 
12:482:23792:17:16:72:526:372:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the  banking  sector,  the  problem  of  non-performing  assets  assumed  a  central  place  in  issues 
12:483:23896:16:17:72:206:356:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:relating to banking sector.   
12:484:23925:17:17:72:75:339:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
12:485:23925:17:17:72:233:322:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:2.1.2 Causes for growing NPA: 
12:486:23954:17:16:90:526:305:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Improper selection of borrowers, inadequacies of character, capacity and capital at the 
12:487:24043:16:18:90:174:289:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:borrower‟s level. 
12:488:24060:18:17:90:395:271:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Deficiencies in appraisal, processing, sanction, and release. 
12:489:24122:17:18:90:513:254:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Inadequate/excess sanction of the limit irrespective of the economic size of the unit. 
12:490:24209:18:17:90:207:236:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Scattered financing. 
12:491:24230:17:18:90:522:219:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Unrealistic terms or conditions of sanction and fixing unrealistic repayment schedule. 
12:492:24317:18:17:90:459:201:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Political interference in sanctioning of loans and patronage to defaulters. 
12:493:24393:17:16:90:526:184:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Lack  of  infrastructural  facilities  like  power,  raw  materials,  fuel,  transportation, 
12:494:24487:16:18:90:250:168:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:marketing and technical support. 
12:495:24519:18:17:90:525:150:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Lack  of  inter-bank  co-ordination  as  well  as  cooperation  with  financial  institution  in 
12:496:24617:17:16:90:316:133:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:exchanging information over list of defaulters. 
12:497:24664:16:17:98:101:117:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
12:498:24664:17:16:98:101:100:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
12:499:24664:16:0:98:101:84:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
13:500:24666:0:16:72:200:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:2.1.3 Objectives of NPA: 
13:501:24690:16:18:72:425:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Management of NPA would have the following three specific objectives: 
13:502:24759:18:16:90:526:724:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Improving the quality of NPA to a performing status so that income on such assets is 
13:503:24845:16:18:90:148:708:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:recognized. 
13:504:24856:18:17:90:495:690:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Upgrading the status of the assets so as to reduce the provisioning requirements. 
13:505:24938:17:17:90:521:673:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Cleansing balance-sheet of loss assets and also unsecured portion of doubtful assets.   
13:506:25026:17:16:72:75:656:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
13:507:25026:16:17:72:207:640:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:2.1.4 Framework of NPA: 
13:508:25049:17:16:72:526:623:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Risk  is  inherent  in  all  aspects  of  a  commercial  operation;  however  for  banks  and  financial 
13:509:25154:16:17:72:526:607:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:institutions,  credit  risk  is  an  essential  factor  that  needs  to  be  managed.  Credit  risk  is  the 
13:510:25263:17:16:72:526:590:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:possibility that a borrower or counter party will fail to meet its obligations in accordance with 
13:511:25360:16:17:72:526:574:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:agreed  terms.  Credit  risk  management  needs  to  be  a  robust  process  that  enables  banks  to 
13:512:25462:17:17:72:526:557:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:proactively  manage  loan  portfolios  in  order to  minimize  losses  and  earn  an  acceptable  level 
13:513:25566:17:16:72:525:540:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of  return  for  shareholders.  And  NPL  management  must  be  thought  of  as  an  integral  part  of 
13:514:25670:16:17:72:526:524:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:overall credit risk management. It implies that NPL management is not an independent event, 
13:515:25762:17:16:72:525:507:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:that  stats  with  conversion  of  a  performing  loan  into  non-performing  loan.  In  fact  a  robust 
13:516:25867:16:17:72:526:491:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:NPL  management  must  start  before  a  loan  becomes  non-performing.  It  is  much  better  to 
13:517:25965:17:185:72:337:474:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:prevent an NPL, rather than curing or nursing an NPL. 
13:518:26018:185:10:486:489:289:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
13:519:26018:10:14:208:389:279:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Figure 1: NPL Management Strategy 
13:520:26051:14:17:72:75:265:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
13:521:26051:17:16:72:526:248:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:NPL  Management  Strategy,  in  figure  2,  explains  that  the  incidence  of  non-performing 
13:522:26146:16:17:72:526:232:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:advances  (NPAs)  is  affecting  the  performance  of  the  credit  institutions  both  financially  and 
13:523:26251:17:16:72:526:215:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:psychologically.  The  successful  banker-client  relationship  in  the  credit  function  of  banks 
13:524:26352:16:18:72:326:199:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:involves three important and interlinked phases viz.: 
13:525:26405:18:17:94:497:181:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The right type and the right amount of credit are given to the right type of client. 
13:526:26489:17:18:94:458:164:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The borrower‟s makes proper use of the amount received from the bank. 
13:527:26559:18:16:94:460:146:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The borrower repays the outstanding loan along with the interest in time. 
13:528:26633:16:18:94:427:130:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Management of NPAs shall rely upon the following basic principles: 
13:529:26699:18:17:94:302:112:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Recovery of normal loans and advances 
13:530:26737:17:0:94:201:95:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Recovery of NPAs 
14:531:26756:0:16:94:526:757:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Compromise  should  be  a  negotiated  settlement  under  which  banks  should  ensure 
14:532:26844:16:18:94:352:741:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:recovery of maximum dues with minimum expenses. 
14:533:26891:18:16:94:526:723:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Proper  distinction  needs  to  be  made  between  willful  defaulters  and  borrowers  who 
14:534:26984:16:18:94:349:707:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:defaulted due to circumstances beyond their control. 
14:535:27036:18:16:94:526:689:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: In settlement cases the banks should promptly recycle the fund with advantage instead 
14:536:27123:16:17:94:450:673:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of resorting to expensive recovery proceedings spread over a long period. 
14:537:27196:17:16:94:97:656:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
14:538:27196:16:17:94:526:640:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:When  the  bank  is  entering  into  compromise  settlement  the  following  points  need  to  be 
14:539:27294:17:17:94:160:623:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:remembered: 
14:540:27305:17:18:94:305:606:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Maximum recovery with minimum cost. 
14:541:27341:18:16:94:526:588:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Distinction  needs to be made between willful defaulters and defaulters on account of 
14:542:27428:16:18:94:244:572:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:conditions beyond their scope. 
14:543:27458:18:16:94:526:554:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Where   security   is available,   proper   weightage   needs   to   be   given   location, 
14:544:27551:16:18:94:312:538:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:marketability conditions, possession thereof. 
14:545:27596:18:16:94:526:520:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Fund  recycling  to  maximum  advantage  instead  of  opting  for  lengthy,  expensive 
14:546:27684:16:18:94:181:504:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:recovery process. 
14:547:27701:18:16:94:526:486:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: All compromise proposals should be reported to the next higher authority for scrutiny 
14:548:27788:16:18:94:274:470:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:so as to prevent fraudulent activities. 
14:549:27827:18:16:94:526:452:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Before   presenting   the   compromise   proposal   before   the   Settlement   Advisory 
14:550:27917:16:18:94:422:436:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:committee, the proposal needs to be examined by the top executive. 
14:551:27983:18:16:94:526:418:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Special  recovery  cells  needs  to  be  set  up  to  monitor  recovery  and  prevent  fresh 
14:552:28077:16:18:94:191:402:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:generation of NPA. 
14:553:28095:18:16:94:526:384:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Adequate  attention  should  be  given  and  appropriate  action  initiated  for  upgrading 
14:554:28188:16:17:94:276:368:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:substandard assets to standard assets. 
14:555:28226:17:16:72:75:351:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
14:556:28226:16:17:72:526:335:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:As a Preventive measure there should have proper screening before disbursement of the 
14:557:28312:17:17:72:252:318:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Loans and surveillance such as:      
14:558:28348:17:18:94:234:301:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To select right borrowers. 
14:559:28375:18:17:94:260:283:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To identify viability of project. 
14:560:28409:17:18:94:267:266:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To ascertain credit environment. 
14:561:28442:18:17:94:215:248:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To assess credit need. 
14:562:28465:17:17:94:239:231:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To timely supply of credit. 
14:563:28493:17:18:94:243:214:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To obtain proper securities. 
14:564:28522:18:17:94:287:196:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To prevent defective documentation. 
14:565:28558:17:17:94:252:179:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To maintain credit discipline. 
14:566:28589:17:16:94:97:162:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
14:567:28589:16:17:72:526:146:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Recovery of credit largely depends on effective follow-up. By supervision we mean to have a 
14:568:28681:17:16:72:525:129:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:proper control over the borrowers operation to ensure the end-use of funds. Supervision keeps 
14:569:28775:16:17:72:526:113:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:track of  the  end-use  of  fund  lent.  Supervision  and  follow-up  function  in  banks  has  assumed 
14:570:28879:17:17:72:455:96:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:considerable significance due to increasing trend of sickness in industrial units. 
14:571:28961:17:0:72:75:79:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
15:572:28963:0:16:72:146:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Loan Review: 
15:573:28975:16:17:72:526:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Loan review  is  not luxury  but necessary  for a sound  bank  lending program. The structure of 
15:574:29072:17:16:72:526:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:credit  review  process would  have  to  periodically  examine  the  assumptions  on  which  every 
15:575:29171:16:17:72:526:709:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:loan  was  appraised  and  granted,  and  whether  these  assumptions  have  changed  materially 
15:576:29268:17:16:72:526:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:enough to endanger the debt-servicing capacity of the borrower. Typically, all or most of the 
15:577:29362:16:17:72:399:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:following aspects are reviewed for every loan till it is repaid in full. 
15:578:29434:17:18:72:75:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
15:579:29434:18:16:90:526:641:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Developments  in the economy that  may  have an  impact on the  industry  in which the 
15:580:29522:16:18:90:183:625:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:borrower operates. 
15:581:29540:18:17:90:452:607:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Developments in the industry or sector in which the borrower operates. 
15:582:29611:17:17:90:405:590:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The borrower‟s payment record in this and other loans so far. 
15:583:29673:17:18:90:450:573:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman:  The quality, condition and value of the prime and collateral securities. 
15:584:29746:18:16:90:526:555:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The  completeness  of  loan  documentation,  and  developments  in  law  governing  the 
15:585:29835:16:18:90:270:539:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:instruments effecting credit delivery. 
15:586:29873:18:16:90:526:521:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Some  borrowers  may  default  on  debt  service  due  to  factors  out  of  their  control.  In 
15:587:29971:16:17:90:526:505:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:such cases, the bank may have to reschedule the debt requirements and alter some of the 
15:588:30059:17:16:90:207:488:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:covenants, if necessary. 
15:589:30083:16:17:72:75:472:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
15:590:30083:17:16:72:526:455:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Central  banks  of  most  countries  have  devised  country-specific  definitions  and  control 
15:591:30179:16:17:72:526:439:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:systems to tackle „sick‟ borrowers. There are three categories of sickness that could afflict 
15:592:30273:17:17:72:127:422:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:borrowers: 
15:593:30283:17:16:94:525:405:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:a) Sickness  at  birth- the  project  itself  has  become  infeasible  either  due  to  faculty 
15:594:30377:16:17:94:294:389:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:assumptions or a change in environment. 
15:595:30416:17:16:94:479:372:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:b) Induced sickness- caused by management in competencies or willful default. 
15:596:30491:16:17:94:526:356:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:c) Genuine   sickness-where   the   circumstances   leading   to   sickness   are   beyond   the 
15:597:30587:17:16:94:525:339:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:borrower‟s control, and has happened in spite of the borrowers sincere efforts to avert 
15:598:30675:16:17:94:159:323:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the situation. 
15:599:30689:17:17:72:75:306:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
15:600:30689:17:17:72:227:289:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Key Steps for Loan Workout: 
15:601:30716:17:17:98:526:272:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Always  keep  the  goal  of  loan  workouts  firmly  in  mind:  to  maximize  the  banks 
15:602:30806:17:17:98:281:255:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:chances for full recovery of its funds. 
15:603:30845:17:17:98:526:238:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The  repaid  detection  and  reporting  of  any  problems  with  a  loan  are  essential;  delay 
15:604:30943:17:17:98:291:221:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:often worsens a problem loan situation. 
15:605:30982:17:17:98:526:204:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Keep  the  loan  workouts  responsibility  separate  from  the  lending  function  to  avoid 
15:606:31076:17:17:98:324:187:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:possible conflicts of interest for the loan offer. 
15:607:31126:17:17:98:526:170:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Bank  workout  specialists  should  confer  with  the  troubled  customer  quickly  on 
15:608:31214:17:16:98:526:153:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:possible  options,  especially  for  cutting  expenses,  increasing cash  flow,  and  improving 
15:609:31309:16:18:98:203:137:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:management control. 
15:610:31328:18:16:98:526:119:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Develop  a  preliminary  plan  of  action  after  determining  the  banks  risk  exposure  and 
15:611:31424:16:17:98:525:103:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:sufficiency of loan documents especially any claims against the customer‟s collateral 
15:612:31510:17:0:98:257:86:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:other than that held by the bank. 
16:613:31545:0:16:98:525:757:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Estimate  what  resources  are  available  to  collect  the  trouble  loan  including  the 
16:614:31637:16:17:98:346:741:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:estimated liquidation values of assets and deposits. 
16:615:31689:17:16:72:75:724:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
16:616:31689:16:18:72:246:708:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Loan review helps in the following: 
16:617:31724:18:17:98:403:690:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Continuously checking if the loan policy is being adhered to. 
16:618:31786:17:18:98:383:673:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Identifying problem accounts even at the incipient stage. 
16:619:31844:18:16:98:324:655:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Assessing the bank‟s exposure to credit risk. 
16:620:31890:16:17:72:75:639:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
16:621:31890:17:14:72:468:622:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:22..22  Objectives and Importance’s of Loan Classification and Provisioning::  
16:622:31965:14:13:72:75:608:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:  
16:623:31965:13:17:72:526:595:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:According to BRPD Circular No. 19 dated December 27, 2012, Bangladesh Bank has, over 
16:624:32050:17:16:72:526:578:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the last several years, positioned the banks on a path towards higher regulatory capital ratios 
16:625:32146:16:17:72:526:562:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:and a more precise calculation of each individual bank‟s need for capital, through a gradual 
16:626:32239:17:16:72:526:545:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:implementation of internationally recognized capital standards. The enforcement of a stricter 
16:627:32333:16:17:72:526:529:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:regulatory  capital  regime  also  requires  measures  to  improve  the  accuracy  of  financial  data 
16:628:32436:17:17:72:526:512:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:which   are  used   internally,  stated  in  the  audited   financial   statements  and  reported  to 
16:629:32538:17:16:72:527:495:12:Times New Roman:12:g_d0_f9:Bangladesh  Bank  as  per  rules.  For  both  the  banks  managerial  and  Bangladesh  Bank‟s 
16:630:32632:16:17:72:526:479:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:supervisory  purposes,  as  well  as  for  accurate  valuation  of  a  bank‟s  capital  in  all  of  its 
16:631:32737:17:16:72:216:462:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:financial reports is necessary. 
16:632:32768:16:14:72:75:446:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
16:633:32768:14:17:72:526:432:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:An accurate valuation of capital relies,  in turn, on an accurate valuation of assets. Loan  loss 
16:634:32866:17:16:72:526:415:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:provisioning – the recognition that some or all of the required payments on a loan may never 
16:635:32958:16:17:72:525:399:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:be  made – is  the  single  most  important  aspect  of  asset  valuation  to  bankers  and  bank 
16:636:33055:17:16:72:526:382:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:supervisors. It is  important because  loans typically  make up 50% or  more of the total assets 
16:637:33152:16:17:72:525:366:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of the bank. Basel II and Basel III devote a great deal of attention to the distinction between 
16:638:33248:17:17:72:526:349:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:“expected  losses” and  “unexpected  losses” on the  bank‟s  loan portfolio. The purpose of 
16:639:33340:17:16:72:527:332:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:provisioning is to take into account expected losses. Expected losses can be assigned to loans 
16:640:33435:16:17:72:526:316:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:based on a loan classification system, which has been utilized in Bangladesh for many years 
16:641:33527:17:16:72:261:299:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:and is being updated with this circular. 
16:642:33567:16:17:72:75:283:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
16:643:33567:17:16:72:526:266:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Bangladesh  Bank  also  wishes  to  stress  that  it  is  the  responsibility  of  bank  management  to 
16:644:33671:16:17:72:525:250:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:adopt  and  implement  proper  accounting  and  reporting,  and  that  correct  classification  and 
16:645:33771:17:16:72:526:233:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:provisioning  is  a  part  of  that  responsibility.  Loan  classification  and  provisioning  must  be  a 
16:646:33878:16:17:72:526:217:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:key  component of  a  regular  internal  loan  review  process that  looks  at the  current  likelihood 
16:647:33982:17:17:72:526:200:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:that  the borrower  will  repay.  The  value  of  the  formed  allowance  that  results  from  the 
16:648:34081:17:16:72:491:183:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:provisioning process should reflect all expected losses resulting from credit exposures. 
16:649:34169:16:17:72:75:167:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
16:650:34169:17:16:72:526:150:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Bangladesh  Bank  has  established  requirements  for  general  loan  loss  provisions,  in  certain 
16:651:34269:16:17:72:526:134:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:percentages,  for  certain  categories  of  loans  that  are  unclassified  or  in  the  Special  Mention 
16:652:34375:17:16:72:526:117:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Account.  As  the  name  suggests,  general  provisions  are  assigned  to  take  into  account  the 
16:653:34476:16:17:72:526:101:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:expected  losses  on  pools  of  loans  that  are  thought  to  have  similar  characteristics.  The 
16:654:34577:17:0:72:526:84:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:characteristics  of  each  individual  loan  are  not  analyzed.  Put  differently,  it  is  not  known  or 
17:655:34687:0:16:72:526:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:even  assumed which  loan or  loans  in the pool are going to result  in  loan  losses;  it  is simply 
17:656:34790:16:17:72:526:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:taken  as  given  that  in  such  large  pools,  even  those  currently  unclassified,  there  will 
17:657:34890:17:16:72:526:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:undoubtedly be individual loans that in the future will not be repaid. Ideally, the percentages 
17:658:34986:16:17:72:526:709:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of provision that are applied to each pool are determined based on historical  loss experience 
17:659:35081:17:16:72:526:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of similar  loan pools. Banks  are encouraged to calculate these  historical  loss experiences on 
17:660:35179:16:17:72:526:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the  loan  pools  for  which  Bangladesh  Bank  has  indicated  general  provision  percentages,  and 
17:661:35281:17:17:72:526:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:use  these  data  if  they  result  in  higher  provisions  than  are  required  in  this  circular.  Because 
17:662:35391:17:16:72:525:642:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:general provisions are not formed based on expectations of loss on any individual loan, they 
17:663:35484:16:17:72:526:626:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:are allowed to be included in the calculation of Tier 2 capital, subject to some restrictions. In 
17:664:35582:17:16:72:526:609:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:contrast,  specific  provisions  (established  on   loans  that  are  classified  as Sub-standard, 
17:665:35681:16:17:72:525:593:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Doubtful  or  Bad/Loss)  are  set  up  on  a  loan-by-loan  basis  after  careful  analysis  of  each 
17:666:35783:17:16:72:526:576:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:individual loan‟s probability of repayment. For loans placed into any of these classification 
17:667:35877:16:17:72:526:560:12:Times New Roman:12:g_d0_f9:categories, weaknesses have been identified that cast doubt on the borrower‟s ability or intent 
17:668:35973:17:17:72:526:543:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:to make all contractual payments in a timely manner. For this reason, specific provisions are 
17:669:36067:17:16:72:370:526:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:not allowed to be included in the calculation of Tier 2 capital. 
17:670:36131:16:17:72:75:510:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
17:671:36131:17:16:72:525:493:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Loan  classification  is  the  act  of  grouping  or  arranging  of  loans  and  advances  according  to 
17:672:36236:16:17:72:526:477:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:their  status  like  unclassified,  sub-standard,  doubtful  and  bad  or  loss  based  on  given  criteria. 
17:673:36345:17:16:72:526:460:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Provisioning  means  setting  aside  certain  fund  from  the  current  year  profit  against  possible 
17:674:36449:16:17:72:525:444:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:loan   losses.   In   Bangladesh,   Bangladesh   bank   prescribes   the   loan   classification   and 
17:675:36552:17:17:72:526:427:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:provisioning criteria through BRPD Circular No. - 1 dated June 05, 2006; BRPD Circular 
17:676:36638:17:16:72:526:410:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:No. -7  June  14,  2012;  BRPD  Circular  No.-14  dated  September  23,  2012  and  BRPD 
17:677:36727:16:17:72:526:394:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Circular No. 19 dated December 27, 2012. As  part of this program, a  new  system of  loan 
17:678:36818:17:16:72:526:377:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:classification  and  provisioning  against  potential  loan  losses  for  advances  was  introduced  in 
17:679:36922:16:17:72:526:361:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:November 1989. Before 1989 no specific guidelines were followed by the commercial banks 
17:680:37010:17:16:72:526:344:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:for  this  purpose.  This  process  is continued  to  date.  The  title  of  the  circular  was “Master 
17:681:37114:16:17:72:526:328:12:g_d0_f14:12:Times New Roman:Circular:  Loan  Classification  and  Provisioning”. The  introduction  of  this  program  was 
17:682:37209:17:16:72:526:311:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:aimed at to bring loan loss provisioning and classification in line with international standards 
17:683:37306:16:17:72:171:295:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:by the end of 2012.  
17:684:37326:17:17:72:75:278:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
17:685:37326:17:16:72:523:261:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Loan  classification  means  giving  each  and  every  loan  case  a  status  like  unclassified,  sub-
17:686:37429:16:17:72:526:245:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:standard, doubtful and bad or loss through verification of borrowers‟ repayment performance 
17:687:37521:17:16:72:526:228:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:on a particular date while provisioning means setting aside fund from the profit (profit before 
17:688:37617:16:17:72:526:212:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:provision and taxes) against possible loan loss. This is obviously essential for determining the 
17:689:37714:17:16:72:526:195:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:financial health and efficiency of the banking sector. Besides, a proper loan classification and 
17:690:37811:16:17:72:526:179:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:provisioning system  ensures credibility of the  financial system that  in turn restores trust and 
17:691:37910:17:17:72:279:162:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:confidence in the minds of the depositors.  
17:692:37953:17:16:72:75:145:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
17:693:37953:16:17:72:526:129:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Loan  classification  makes  two  pronged  attacks  on  the  activities  of  banks. First, interests 
17:694:38054:17:16:72:526:112:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:applied on loans are not taken into account because such interests are to be taken into account 
17:695:38150:16:17:72:526:96:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:only  on  its  realization. Second, banks  have  to  make  provisions  on  classified  loans as  per 
17:696:38251:17:0:72:523:79:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:guidelines by Bangladesh Bank from out of the income earned by them on performing loans.  
18:697:38340:0:17:72:248:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Objectives of Loan Classification: 
18:698:38374:17:18:94:251:741:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Find out net-worth of a bank. 
18:699:38404:18:17:94:347:723:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Help for assessing financial soundness of a bank. 
18:700:38454:17:18:94:477:706:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Help for determining required provision and the amount of interest suspense 
18:701:38530:18:16:94:526:688:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Put  the  bank  on  sound  footing  in  order  to  develop  sound  banking  practice  in 
18:702:38620:16:16:94:156:672:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Bangladesh. 
18:703:38631:16:17:72:75:656:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
18:704:38631:17:17:72:254:639:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Importance of Loan Classification: 
18:705:38665:17:18:94:234:622:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Strength credit discipline, 
18:706:38693:18:17:94:287:604:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Improve loan recovery positions and 
18:707:38729:17:17:94:254:587:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Make future planning of loan  
18:708:38759:17:17:72:77:570:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:  
18:709:38759:17:16:72:273:553:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:2.3 Categories of Loans and Advances: 
18:710:38796:16:17:72:526:537:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:For  the  purpose  of  loan  classification,  loan  and  advances  have  been  grouped  into  four 
18:711:38895:17:16:72:127:520:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:categories: 
18:712:38906:16:17:72:75:504:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
18:713:38906:17:16:72:526:487:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(a) Continuous loan: The loan which is sanctioned without specific repayment  schedule 
18:714:38991:16:17:72:526:471:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:but there is a specific expiry date for repayment and credit limit can be treated as continuous 
18:715:39087:17:17:72:316:454:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:loan. For examples: O/D, CC, PC, LIM, LTR, etc. 
18:716:39134:17:16:72:75:437:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
18:717:39134:16:16:72:526:421:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(b) Demand Loan: When loan is sanctioned on the basis of repayment depends upon the 
18:718:39216:16:17:72:526:405:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:demand  of  bank  can  be  treated  as  demand  loan.  Contingent  or  other  liabilities  which  are 
18:719:39318:17:17:72:526:388:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:converted into forced loan are also to be treated as demand loan. For examples: Forced LIM, 
18:720:39410:17:16:72:174:371:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:PAD, FBP, IBP, etc. 
18:721:39429:16:14:72:75:355:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
18:722:39429:14:16:72:525:341:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(c) Term Loan: The  loan which  has a specific  expiry date for repayment and  for which 
18:723:39517:16:17:72:526:325:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:repayment is schedule through specific repayment schedule is treated as fixed term loan. For 
18:724:39610:17:17:72:330:308:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:example: Project finance, industrial finance, and tec.  
18:725:39665:17:14:72:75:291:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
18:726:39665:14:16:72:526:277:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(d) Short-Term   Agricultural   Credit and   Micro-Credit: Short-Term   Agricultural 
18:727:39748:16:17:72:526:261:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Credit means the credit which is enlisted as short term credit under the annual credit program 
18:728:39843:17:16:72:526:244:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:announced  by  Agricultural  Credit  Department  of  Bangladesh  bank.  Credit  in  agriculture 
18:729:39939:16:17:72:523:228:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:sector repayable within 12 months is also included in this category. On the other hand, Short-
18:730:40033:17:16:72:526:211:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Term  Micro-Credit  means  the  credit  which  have  loan  limit  less  than  TK.  25000.00  and 
18:731:40130:16:17:72:526:195:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:repayable  within  12  months.  Micro-credit  may  be  even  non-farm  credit,  self-employment 
18:732:40226:17:17:72:478:178:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:credit, loom-loan or any forms of credit under the own credit program of the banks.  
18:733:40309:17:17:72:75:161:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
18:734:40309:17:16:72:250:144:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:22..44      Basis for Loan Classification: 
18:735:40345:16:16:72:526:128:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:If  any  uncertainty  or  doubt  arises  in  respect  of  recovery  of  any  Continuous  Loan,  Demand 
18:736:40448:16:17:72:526:112:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Loan  or  Fixed  Term  Loan,  the  same  will  have  to  be  classified  on  the basis  of  qualitative 
18:737:40552:17:16:72:526:95:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:judgement be it classifiable or not on the basis of objective criteria. If any situational changes 
18:738:40651:16:0:72:526:79:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:occur  in  the  stipulations  in  terms  of  which  the  loan  was  extended  or  if  the  capital  of  the 
19:739:40761:0:16:72:526:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:borrower is impaired due to adverse conditions or if the value of the collateral decreases or if 
19:740:40858:16:17:72:526:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the recovery of the loan becomes uncertain due to any other unfavourable situation, the loan 
19:741:40951:17:16:72:380:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:will have to be classified on the basis of qualitative judgement . 
19:742:41017:16:17:72:75:709:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
19:743:41017:17:16:72:525:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Despite the probability of any  loan being affected due to the reasons stated above or for any 
19:744:41112:16:17:72:526:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:other reasons, if there is any hope for change of the existing condition by resorting to proper 
19:745:41208:17:17:72:526:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:steps, the loan, on the basis of qualitative judgement, will be classified as 'Sub-standard '. But 
19:746:41307:17:16:72:526:642:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:even after resorting to proper steps, there exists  no certainty of total recovery of the  loan,  it 
19:747:41407:16:17:72:526:626:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:will  be  classified  as  '  Doubtful  '  and  even  after  exerting  the  all-out  efforts,  there  exists  no 
19:748:41519:17:16:72:526:609:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:chance of recovery, it will be classified as ' Bad/Loss ' on the basis of qualitative judgement. 
19:749:41616:16:17:72:526:593:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:For incorporating qualitative judgment, banks must focus on the likelihood that the borrower 
19:750:41709:17:16:72:526:576:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:will repay  all amounts due  in a timely  manner, using their own  judgment and the  following 
19:751:41804:16:17:72:167:560:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:assessment factors: 
19:752:41823:17:17:72:75:543:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
19:753:41823:17:16:72:178:526:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(1) Special Mention: 
19:754:41843:16:17:72:526:510:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: a)  Assets  must  be  classified  no  higher  than  Special  Mention  if  any  of  the  following 
19:755:41940:17:16:72:526:493:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:deficiencies  of  bank  management  is  present:  the  loan  was  not  made  in  compliance  with  the 
19:756:42042:16:17:72:526:477:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:bank‟s internal policies; failure to maintain adequate and enforceable documentation; or poor 
19:757:42134:17:17:72:184:460:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:control over collateral. 
19:758:42158:17:16:72:75:443:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
19:759:42158:16:16:72:526:427:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:b)  Assets  must  be  classified  no  higher  than  Special  Mention  if  any  of  the  following 
19:760:42256:16:17:72:523:411:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:deficiencies  of  the  obligor  is  present:  occasional  overdrawn  within  the  past  year,  below-
19:761:42357:17:17:72:522:394:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:average or declining profitability; barely acceptable liquidity; problems in strategic planning. 
19:762:42453:17:16:72:75:377:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
19:763:42453:16:17:72:166:361:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(2) Sub-standard: 
19:764:42470:17:16:72:526:344:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:a) Assets must be classified no higher than Sub-standard if any of the following deficiencies 
19:765:42564:16:17:72:526:328:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of the obligor is present: recurrent overdrawn, low account turnover, competitive difficulties, 
19:766:42660:17:16:72:525:311:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:location in a volatile industry with an acute drop in demand; very low profitability that is also 
19:767:42758:16:17:72:526:295:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:declining; inadequate liquidity; cash flow less than repayment of principal and interest; weak 
19:768:42853:17:17:72:526:278:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:management;  doubts  about  integrity  of  management;  conflict  in  corporate  governance; 
19:769:42946:17:16:72:441:261:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:unjustifiable lack of external audit; pending litigation of a significant nature. 
19:770:43027:16:17:72:75:245:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
19:771:43027:17:16:72:526:228:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:b) Assets must be classified no higher than Sub-standard if the primary sources of repayment 
19:772:43120:16:17:72:526:212:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:are insufficient to service the debt and the bank must look to secondary sources of repayment, 
19:773:43215:17:16:72:171:195:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:including collateral. 
19:774:43236:16:17:72:75:179:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
19:775:43236:17:17:72:526:162:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:c)  Assets  must  be  classified  no  higher  than  Sub-standard  if  the  banking  organization  has 
19:776:43338:17:16:72:526:145:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:acquired the asset without the types of adequate documentation of the obligor‟s net worth, 
19:777:43429:16:17:72:525:129:12:Times New Roman:12:g_d0_f9:profitability,  liquidity, and cash flow that are required in the banking organization‟s lending 
19:778:43526:17:16:72:398:112:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:policy, or there are doubts about the validity of that documentation. 
19:779:43595:16:17:72:75:96:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
19:780:43595:17:0:72:75:79:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
20:781:43597:0:16:72:142:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(3) Doubtful: 
20:782:43610:16:17:72:527:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Assets must be classified no higher than Doubtful if any of the following deficiencies of the 
20:783:43704:17:16:72:526:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:obligor is present: permanent overdrawn; location in an industry with poor aggregate earnings 
20:784:43798:16:17:72:526:709:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:or loss of markets; serious competitive problems; failure of key products; operational losses; 
20:785:43893:17:16:72:526:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:illiquidity,  including  the  necessity  to  sell  assets  to  meet  operating  expenses;  cash  flow  less 
20:786:44001:16:17:72:526:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:than   required   interest   payments;   very   poor   management;   non-cooperative   or   hostile 
20:787:44101:17:17:72:526:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:management;  serious  doubts  of  the  integrity  of  management;  doubts  about  true  ownership; 
20:788:44200:17:16:72:312:642:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:complete absence of faith in financial statements. 
20:789:44250:16:17:72:75:626:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
20:790:44250:17:16:72:139:609:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(4) Bad/Loss 
20:791:44262:16:17:72:526:593:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Assets must be classified no higher than Bad/Loss if any of the following deficiencies of the 
20:792:44356:17:16:72:526:576:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:obligor are present: the obligor seeks  new  loans to finance operational  losses;  location  in an 
20:793:44456:16:17:72:526:560:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:industry  that  is  disappearing;  location  in  the  bottom  quartile  of  its  industry  in  terms  of 
20:794:44561:17:17:72:526:543:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:profitability;  technological  obsolescence;  very  high  losses;  asset  sales  at  a  loss  to  meet 
20:795:44664:17:16:72:526:526:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:operational  expenses;  cash  flow  less  than  production  costs;  no  repayment  source  except 
20:796:44762:16:17:72:526:510:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:liquidation;  presence  of  money  laundering,  fraud,  embezzlement,  or  other  criminal  activity; 
20:797:44864:17:17:72:217:493:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:no further support by owners. 
20:798:44893:17:16:72:75:476:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:  
20:799:44893:16:17:72:228:460:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:2.5 Maintenance of Provision::  
20:800:44923:17:16:72:75:443:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:  
20:801:44923:16:16:72:526:427:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:a) General Provision: Banks will be required to maintain General Provision in the following 
20:802:45015:16:17:72:98:411:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:way: 
20:803:45019:17:17:72:75:394:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
20:804:45019:17:16:72:526:377:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(1) @ 0.25% against all unclassified loans of Small and Medium Enterprise (SME) as defined 
20:805:45110:16:17:72:526:361:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:by the SME & Special Programmes Department of Bangladesh Bank  from time to time and 
20:806:45195:17:16:72:526:344:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:@  1%  against  all  unclassified  loans  (other  than  loans  under  Consumer  Financing,  Loans  to 
20:807:45297:16:17:72:526:328:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Brokerage  House,  Merchant  Banks,  Stock  dealers  etc.,  Special  Mention  Account  as  well  as 
20:808:45397:17:16:72:157:311:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:SME Financing.) 
20:809:45412:16:17:72:75:295:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
20:810:45412:17:17:72:526:278:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(2) @ 5% on the unclassified amount for Consumer financing whereas it has to be maintained 
20:811:45503:17:16:72:526:261:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:@ 2% on the unclassified amount for (i) Housing Finance and (ii) Loans for Professionals to 
20:812:45595:16:17:72:324:245:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:set up business under Consumer Financing Scheme. 
20:813:45643:17:16:72:75:228:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
20:814:45643:16:17:72:526:212:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(3) @ 2% on the unclassified amount for Loans to Brokerage House, Merchant Banks, Stock 
20:815:45731:17:16:72:131:195:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:dealers, etc. 
20:816:45744:16:17:72:75:179:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
20:817:45744:17:17:72:480:162:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(4) @ 5% on the outstanding amount of loans kept in the 'Special Mention Account'. 
20:818:45826:17:16:72:75:145:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
20:819:45826:16:17:72:526:129:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(5)  @1%  on  the  off-balance  sheet  exposures.  (Provision  will  be  on  the  total  exposure  and 
20:820:45929:17:16:72:526:112:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:amount  of  cash  margin  or  value  of  eligible  collateral  will  not  be  deducted  while  computing 
20:821:46034:16:17:72:213:96:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Off-balance sheet exposure.) 
20:822:46062:17:0:72:75:79:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
21:823:46064:0:16:72:526:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:b)  Specific  Provision: Banks  will  maintain  provision  at  the  following  rates  in  respect  of 
21:824:46166:16:17:72:340:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:classified Continuous, Demand and Fixed Term Loans: 
21:825:46217:17:16:72:183:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(1) Sub-standard: 20% 
21:826:46238:16:17:72:163:709:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(2) Doubtful: 50% 
21:827:46255:17:16:72:171:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(3) Bad/Loss: 100% 
21:828:46273:16:17:72:75:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
21:829:46273:17:17:72:384:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:c) Provision for Short-term Agricultural and Micro-Credits: 
21:830:46332:17:16:72:509:642:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(1) All credits except 'Bad/Loss' (i.e. 'Doubtful', 'Sub-standard', irregular and regular credit 
21:831:46429:16:17:72:143:626:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:accounts): 5% 
21:832:46442:17:17:72:186:609:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:(2) 'Bad/Loss‟   : 100% 
21:833:46465:17:17:72:75:592:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:  
21:834:46465:17:15:72:135:575:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:TToo  SSuumm  uupp::  
21:835:46481:15:17:72:526:560:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:The  base  for  provisions  on  non-performing  loans  was  the  balance  outstanding  in  the  loan 
21:836:46582:17:17:72:526:543:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:ledger for the loan, less any interest taken in an interest suspense account.  However, the base 
21:837:46679:17:16:72:526:526:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:for  provision  shall  be  further  reviewed  towards  closer  convergence  with  international  best 
21:838:46781:16:17:72:164:510:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:practice standards. 
21:839:46800:17:24:72:75:493:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:

21:841:46824:0:14:350:453:476:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Required Provision

21:844:46895:18:17:108:409:428:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Substandard 1 year < 3 years 10

21:848:46972:14:13:72:290:363:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:          Source:  BRPD circular no. 07 / 2012  
21:849:47019:13:14:72:75:350:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
21:850:47019:14:17:72:526:336:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:In  latest BRPD  circular  no.  19  dated  December  27,  2012,  an  amended  and  revised  loan 
21:851:47116:17:17:72:526:319:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:classification and provisioning procedure was introduced by the Bangladesh Bank to bring it 
21:852:47207:17:16:72:526:302:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:in  line  with  the  international  standards.  This  was  implemented  in  five  phases,  the  last  of 
21:853:47312:16:17:72:526:286:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:which ended in December 2012. In the revised policy, the duration for loans to be classified 
21:854:47405:17:16:72:526:269:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:under  various  categories  was  drastically  reduced,  while  the  frequency  of  classifications  was 
21:855:47509:16:17:72:526:253:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:increased.  For  classification  and  provisioning  under  the  revised  procedure  banks  were 
21:856:47605:17:16:72:336:236:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:instructed to classify the loans in following procedure: 
21:857:47661:16:27:72:75:220:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
21:858:47661:27:0:127:305:193:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Loans Duration of overdue 
21:859:47685:0:14:347:450:200:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Required Provision

21:867:47884:14:0:72:75:82:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
22:868:47886:0:16:72:526:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:According  to BRPD  circular  no.  19  dated  December  27,  2012 either  of  these  continuous, 
22:869:47982:16:17:72:508:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:demand and fixed term loans will be classifying and provisioning by following procedure: 
22:870:48070:17:22:72:75:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
22:871:48070:22:0:127:303:703:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Loans Duration of overdue

22:880:48276:14:16:108:111:594:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
22:881:48276:16:17:72:195:578:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:2.6 Loan Rescheduling: 
22:882:48298:17:16:72:526:561:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Latest BRPD  circular  no.  19  dated  December  27,  2012, Bangladesh  Bank  recognizes  that 
22:883:48393:16:17:72:526:545:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:in  some cases, a  legitimate banking practice  may  allow  for the renewal of a continuous  loan 
22:884:48491:17:16:72:526:528:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:or  line  of  credit.  Occasionally,  even  a  term  loan  is  renewed  or  extended  under  unfortunate 
22:885:48596:16:17:72:526:512:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:circumstances  that  are  beyond  the  control  of  the  borrower  and  do  not  signify  that  the 
22:886:48696:17:17:72:526:495:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:borrower's  willingness  or  ability  to  repay  has  deteriorated  the  loan.  However,  Bangladesh 
22:887:48797:17:16:72:526:478:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:Bank is concerned that rescheduling (also known as “prolongation” or “evergreening”) may 
22:888:48886:16:17:72:526:462:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:sometimes  result  in  an  overstatement  of  capital,  when  loans  that  have  a  low  probability  of 
22:889:48991:17:16:72:526:445:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:repayment  are  carried  at  full  value  on  banks'  balance  sheets.  Bangladesh  Bank  is  hereby 
22:890:49092:16:17:72:526:429:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:issuing  this  circular  in  order  to  communicate  its  policy  stance  that  rescheduling  should  be 
22:891:49197:17:17:72:353:412:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:done only in limited circumstances and under restrictions. 
22:892:49255:17:13:72:75:395:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:

24:1071:53223:17:16:72:75:430:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:
