52:2496:117451:14:13:217:515:253:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:quality  of  the  loan  portfolio  which  is  expected  to  transpire 
52:2497:117521:13:14:217:515:240:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:due  to  the  rapid  credit  expansion  in  recent  years.  However, 
52:2498:117590:14:14:217:515:226:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the  classified  loans  of  the  banking  sector  actually  fell  to  6.2 
52:2499:117664:14:14:217:515:212:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:percent from 7.1 percent, a decrease by 0.9 percentage points 
52:2500:117726:14:15:217:415:198:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:as at end-2011 compared with end-2010. 
52:2501:117764:15:13:217:515:183:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The  classified  loans  to  total  loans  ratio  has  decreased  to 
52:2502:117833:13:14:217:515:170:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:6.2 percent in CY11 from 7.1 percent in CY10. Bad loans to 
52:2503:117892:14:14:217:515:156:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:total classified loans ratio decreased to 73.8 percent in CY11 
52:2504:117955:14:14:217:515:142:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:from 86.1 percent in CY10, still it shows significant inferior 
52:2505:118018:14:14:217:386:128:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:asset quality of the banking sector. 
52:2506:118054:14:14:217:220:114:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
52:2507:118054:14:14:86:166:100:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Recent Reform 
52:2508:118067:14:0:86:170:86:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Initiatives, 2012 
52:2509:118084:0:14:216:515:99:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Banks desirous of financing the purchase of used vehicles 
52:2510:118143:14:0:217:515:85:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:shall prepare uniform guidelines for determining value of the 
53:2511:118207:0:15:100:443:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Name of Measure NPL Management Guidelines 
53:2512:118247:15:13:217:515:743:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:used  vehicles.  However,  the  bank  shall  only  finance  the 
53:2513:118311:13:14:217:514:730:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:vehicles  imported as described  in the existing Import Policy 
53:2514:118374:14:15:217:251:716:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Order. 
53:2515:118380:15:13:216:514:701:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Loan-margin  ratio  for  fresh  loans  shall  be  maintained  at 
53:2516:118446:13:14:217:515:688:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:70:30 in case of house finance under consumer financing and 
53:2517:118506:14:14:217:513:674:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:30:70 for all other consumer loans including motor car loans. 
53:2518:118567:14:15:217:220:660:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
53:2519:118567:15:13:86:172:645:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Other Measures 
53:2520:118581:13:0:86:89:632:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
53:2521:118581:0:14:217:514:645:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Banks with net classified  loans of up to five per cent are 
53:2522:118641:14:14:217:515:631:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:allowed  to  sanction  a  maximum  of  56  percent  of  total  loans 
53:2523:118710:14:15:217:366:617:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:and advances as “large loans". 
53:2524:118740:15:13:217:514:602:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Banks with  net classified  loans between  five percent and 
53:2525:118801:13:14:217:515:589:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:ten  percent  are  allowed  to  lend  52  percent  of  their  portfolio 
53:2526:118873:14:15:217:299:575:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:as “large loans”. 
53:2527:118890:15:14:217:514:560:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Banks   with   net  classified   loans   between  10   and  15 
53:2528:118954:14:14:217:515:546:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:percent  are  allowed  to  lend  up  to  48  percent  of  their  total 
53:2529:119025:14:14:217:327:532:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:loans as “large loans”. 
53:2530:119048:14:14:217:514:518:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Banks  with  net  classified  loans  of  20  percent  and  more 
53:2531:119113:14:14:217:515:504:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:are  allowed  to  lend  a  maximum  of  44  percent  of their  total 
53:2532:119182:14:14:217:327:490:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:loans as “large loans”. 
53:2533:119205:14:14:217:514:476:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The  Bangladesh  Bank  has  also  advised  the  banks  pursue 
53:2534:119268:14:15:217:456:462:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:“syndicated loans” in case of large loan amounts. 
53:2535:119317:15:14:217:514:447:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: An incentive package for bank officials of NCBs to speed 
53:2536:119375:14:13:217:515:433:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:up  the  recovery  of  default  loans.  NCB  staff  receives  seven 
53:2537:119443:13:14:217:515:420:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:percent of the  loan  for  helping the  bank to recover any  loan 
53:2538:119509:14:14:217:515:406:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:which  remained  unrealized  for  seven  years  or  more  and  has 
53:2539:119576:14:14:217:515:392:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:already been labelled as a “bad debt”. In case of recovery of 
53:2540:119638:14:14:217:515:378:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:bad debts that remain unrealized for three to seven years, the 
53:2541:119701:14:14:217:515:364:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:staff  would receive  six  percent  of  the  amount,  while  they 
53:2542:119767:14:13:217:515:350:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:would  receive  five  percent  of  the  amount  as  incentive  for 
53:2543:119834:13:14:217:515:337:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:realizing other bad loans. Besides, bank staff would get four 
53:2544:119896:14:14:217:515:323:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:percent  in  case  of  realization  of  “doubtful  loans”.  The 
53:2545:119960:14:14:217:514:309:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:incentives would be given on an yearly basis upon closure of 
53:2546:120021:14:14:217:292:295:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:a loan account. 
53:2547:120036:14:14:217:514:281:12:g_d0_f11:12:g_d0_f9: “Habitual”  defaulters  are  prohibited  from  getting  any 
53:2548:120097:14:15:217:345:267:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:loan rescheduling facility. 
53:2549:120124:15:14:217:514:252:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Bangladesh    Bank    retains    the    right    to    check    the 
53:2550:120193:14:13:217:515:238:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:transaction  of  a  bank  and  to  impose  a  penalty  if  it  finds 
53:2551:120262:13:14:217:514:225:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:doubtful transactions and subsequently proves malpractice of 
53:2552:120323:14:14:217:268:211:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the banks. 
53:2553:120333:14:17:72:75:197:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
53:2554:120333:17:17:72:75:180:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
53:2555:120333:17:16:72:75:163:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
53:2556:120333:16:17:108:111:147:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
53:2557:120333:17:0:72:75:130:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
54:2558:120335:0:14:72:75:717:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
54:2559:120335:14:14:72:259:703:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:6.1 Causes of Loan Default Problem 
54:2560:120369:14:13:72:75:689:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
54:2561:120369:13:14:72:211:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:A. Entrepreneurs Related: 
54:2562:120394:14:14:72:160:662:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:A1: Young Age:  
54:2563:120409:14:16:72:526:648:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Young  age  is  one  of  the  reasons  behind  the  failure  of payment  of  regular  loan.  Because  of 
54:2564:120513:16:17:72:526:632:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:young age people  suffer  from  lack of  business experience. On the other hand they  normally 
54:2565:120608:17:16:72:526:615:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:don‟t have enough banking experience. As they are young and lack experience, it may be one 
54:2566:120699:16:17:72:220:599:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of the reasons of default loan.  
54:2567:120731:17:17:72:75:582:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
54:2568:120731:17:16:72:250:565:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:A2: Lack of Business Experience:  
54:2569:120764:16:17:72:526:549:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Sometimes people without prior business experience want to do something. It may so happen 
54:2570:120854:17:16:72:526:532:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:that after retirement from govt. or private service people want to establish a business which is 
54:2571:120951:16:17:72:526:516:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:not very relevant to his past experience. Besides  his own equity they  look  for bank  finance. 
54:2572:121048:17:16:72:526:499:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Normally  banks  do  not  finance  in  the  projects  where the  key  personnel  do  not  have  enough 
54:2573:121151:16:17:72:526:483:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:background  in  that  particular  business.  When  banks  finance  in  the  projects  where  the  key 
54:2574:121253:17:16:72:526:466:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:personnel  lack  relevant business  experience,  it  becomes  risky  for  the  bank.  Probability  of 
54:2575:121355:16:17:72:320:450:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:failure in these sorts of projects tends to be higher.  
54:2576:121410:17:17:72:75:433:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
54:2577:121410:17:16:72:432:416:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:A3: Lack of Business and Lack of Institutional Training Background: 
54:2578:121477:16:17:72:526:400:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Business  experience  is  somehow  related to  business  background.  Here  business  background 
54:2579:121574:17:16:72:526:383:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:means  family  business  background.  Though  family  business  has  a  role  in  entrepreneurial 
54:2580:121672:16:17:72:526:367:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:orientation,  there   is   no  direct  relationship  between   business   background  and  business 
54:2581:121772:17:16:72:526:350:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:performance or  loan repayment. It is true that  youths coming  from  business  background are 
54:2582:121867:16:17:72:526:334:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:familiar with business and banking but there are other ways to get oriented with the same, not 
54:2583:121962:17:17:72:319:317:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:necessarily one has to come from business family.  
54:2584:122012:17:16:72:75:300:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
54:2585:122012:16:17:72:207:284:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:A4: Unwillingness to Pay: 
54:2586:122037:17:16:72:526:267:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:We all know this is one of the most common reasons behind default culture in Bangladesh. It 
54:2587:122129:16:17:72:526:251:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:can  happen  in  some  situations  like  when  security  backing  loan  is  weak,  customer  feels  that 
54:2588:122234:17:16:72:526:234:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:defaulting  the  loan  will  not  harm  him  much.  In  that  case  he  tends  to  default.  In  other  cases 
54:2589:122344:16:17:72:526:218:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:like  when  cash  flow  from  the  business  is  not  impressive,  people  are  unwilling  to  repay  the 
54:2590:122450:17:16:72:526:201:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:loans.   Even   sometimes   without   any   reason   customers   default   loan   that   is   purely 
54:2591:122551:16:17:72:346:185:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:psychological and absolute unwillingness to repay loan.  
54:2592:122607:17:17:72:75:168:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
54:2593:122607:17:16:72:249:151:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:A5: Lack of Supporting Facilities: 
54:2594:122641:16:17:72:526:135:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Sometimes business need support from other sources. When cash flow is lean and the project 
54:2595:122732:17:16:72:526:118:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:is in lull, it needs feeding. Without further feeding company may become sick and incur loss 
54:2596:122825:16:0:72:526:102:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:in consecutive time periods. In our country most of the companies do not have the supporting 
54:2597:122918:0:14:249:318:759:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Chapter- Six 
54:2598:122929:14:14:282:285:745:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
54:2599:122929:14:0:131:435:731:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Identify the Causes and Remedies of non-performing loans 
55:2600:122987:0:16:72:525:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:sources with which they  can withstand the turmoil that comes  in to their  business  from time 
55:2601:123083:16:17:72:111:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:to time. 
55:2602:123091:17:17:72:75:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
55:2603:123091:17:16:72:180:708:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:B: Business Related:  
55:2604:123111:16:16:72:224:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:B1: Non Attractive Industry: 
55:2605:123139:16:17:72:526:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Sometimes no attractive industry acts as primary cause of loan default. Companies operating 
55:2606:123231:17:17:72:526:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:in  non  attractive  industries  have  higher  probability  of  performing  poor.  Because  of  poor 
55:2607:123332:17:16:72:526:642:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:financial performance, company‟s cash flow gets affected. Because of cash flow the company 
55:2608:123423:16:17:72:526:626:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:becomes  less  liquid  which  contributes  in  defaulting  bank  loan.  Not  necessarily  that  all  the 
55:2609:123528:17:16:72:322:609:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:companies of non attractive industry perform poor.  
55:2610:123579:16:17:72:75:593:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
55:2611:123579:17:16:72:201:576:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:B2: Strong Competition: 
55:2612:123602:16:17:72:526:560:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Strong  competition  does  not  directly  contribute  in  defaulting  loan.  Strong  competition  takes 
55:2613:123706:17:17:72:526:543:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:place when  many  companies enter  into an  industry where the  industry cannot accommodate 
55:2614:123797:17:16:72:526:526:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:so  many  companies.  In  strong  competition  only  efficient  players  survive.  So  the  inefficient 
55:2615:123901:16:17:72:526:510:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:companies find it difficult to make profit and sale their product. Once they fail to make profit, 
55:2616:123999:17:16:72:380:493:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the company is likely to default its loan installment in the bank. 
55:2617:124065:16:17:72:75:477:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
55:2618:124065:17:16:72:251:460:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:B3: Poor Management Capability: 
55:2619:124096:16:17:72:526:444:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Before  sanctioning  a  loan  banks  look  in  to  the  matter  that  how  the  management  of  the 
55:2620:124196:17:16:72:526:427:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:company is. If the bank feels that the management is capable enough to successfully run the 
55:2621:124288:16:17:72:526:411:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:business and utilize bank finance, then bank agree to finance otherwise not. Even sometimes 
55:2622:124379:17:17:72:526:394:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:banks  sets  conditions  like  some  of  the  key  personnel  must  not  quit  the  organization  before 
55:2623:124484:17:16:72:526:377:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:repayment  of  the  loan.  Managerial  capability  plays  a  vital  role  in  repaying  bank  loan.  The 
55:2624:124589:16:17:72:443:361:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:more professional the management is the less probability of defaulting loan.  
55:2625:124666:17:17:72:75:344:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
55:2626:124666:17:16:72:245:327:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:B4: Poor Financial Performance: 
55:2627:124697:16:16:72:526:311:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Definitely  Poor  financial  performance  is  the  most  important  cause  of  loan  default.  Once  a 
55:2628:124800:16:17:72:526:295:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:company is not solvent, it is un-likely to repay its loan. Poor financial performance is the key 
55:2629:124897:17:17:72:526:278:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:reason  behind  maximum  loan  default.  Poor  financial  performance  can  be  arisen  from  many 
55:2630:124996:17:16:72:222:261:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:other reasons described above. 
55:2631:125026:16:17:108:111:245:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
55:2632:125026:17:16:72:178:228:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:B5: Poor Cash flow: 
55:2633:125045:16:17:72:526:212:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:In most cases poor cash flow is the aftermath of poor financial performance. Because of poor 
55:2634:125138:17:16:72:526:195:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:cash  flow companies  mainly default  loan. Because of  irregular cash  flow, business  becomes 
55:2635:125234:16:17:72:526:179:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:unstable  and  illiquid.  In  that  case  business  does  not  have  enough  cash  to  service  loans 
55:2636:125336:17:17:72:526:162:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:payment and  interest. Even  if a company  is profitable, the company  may  default  because of 
55:2637:125431:17:16:72:526:145:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:cash flow. In some cases, a business may sell  most of its finished goods in credit. So it may 
55:2638:125526:16:17:72:471:129:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:not have enough cash to support the loan and other debts. So it may cause default.  
55:2639:125609:17:16:72:75:112:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
55:2640:125609:16:17:72:75:96:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
55:2641:125609:17:0:72:75:79:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
56:2642:125611:0:16:72:190:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:B6: Low market share 
56:2643:125631:16:17:72:526:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Low market share may be a reason of loan default but not a single respondent mentioned it as 
56:2644:125724:17:16:72:526:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:one of the reasons of their  loan default. Low  market share  means  low  sales,  low sales  mean 
56:2645:125822:16:17:72:526:709:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:low profit and  low profit results default. But operating  in a  niche  market, having a  very  low 
56:2646:125922:17:16:72:526:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:market  share  a  firm  can  be  profitable  enough  to  repay  its  entire  loan  obligation  as  well  as 
56:2647:126030:16:17:72:183:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:retain sizable earning.  
56:2648:126054:17:17:72:75:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
56:2649:126054:17:16:72:179:642:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:CC::  Lending Related: 
56:2650:126074:16:17:72:294:626:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:C1: Delayed Assessment of Loan Proposal: 
56:2651:126114:17:16:72:526:609:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Banks  sometimes  make  delay  in  assessing  loan  proposals  of  the  business  firms.  When  the 
56:2652:126214:16:17:72:525:593:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:firm badly needs money, it does not get enough funds because of delayed assessment by the 
56:2653:126304:17:16:72:526:576:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:bank.  This  infuses  shortage  of  cash  in  their  business  operations.  They  hardly  manage  their 
56:2654:126408:16:17:72:374:560:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:day to day business expenses let alone repayment of the loans. 
56:2655:126470:17:17:72:75:543:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
56:2656:126470:17:16:72:259:526:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:C2: Delayed Disbursement of Fund: 
56:2657:126503:16:17:72:526:510:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Even  after  assessment  of  the  proposal  and  taking  positive  decision,  banks  do  not  disburse 
56:2658:126606:17:16:72:526:493:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:funds until security documentation formalities are completed. As a result business do not get 
56:2659:126700:16:17:72:526:477:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:fund  when  actually  it  requires  it.  Some  of  the  defaulters  complained  about  subsequent 
56:2660:126798:17:16:72:149:460:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:disbursements.  
56:2661:126813:16:17:72:75:444:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
56:2662:126813:17:16:72:240:427:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:C3: Lack of Proper Monitoring: 
56:2663:126843:16:17:72:526:411:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Monitoring is one of the most important parts in credit. Through monitoring lenders come to 
56:2664:126935:17:17:72:526:394:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:know  that  whether  their  fund  is  being  used  for  the  desired  purpose  or  not.  Sometimes 
56:2665:127034:17:16:72:526:377:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:disbursed  money  is  used  for  purposes  other than  the  specific  areas.  In  that  case  risk  of  loan 
56:2666:127143:16:17:72:526:361:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:default  gets  higher.  Banks  sanction  loan  on  the  basis  of  feasibility  of  the  project.  Bank  as  a 
56:2667:127254:17:16:72:526:344:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:lender  expect  that  the  loan  will  be  serviced  by  the  cash  flow  generated  from  that  particular 
56:2668:127362:16:17:72:526:328:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:business. But if credit  is used  in some other areas desired cash  flow  may  not come  from the 
56:2669:127460:17:16:72:526:311:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:business  and  chance  of  loan  default  gets  high.  Therefore  banks  monitor  activities  of  the 
56:2670:127562:16:17:72:526:295:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:borrower  whether  the  fund  is  being  properly  utilized  or  business  is  generating  enough  cash 
56:2671:127666:17:17:72:526:278:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:flow or not. Banks use specialized formats for loan monitoring. Bank periodically review the 
56:2672:127759:17:16:72:526:261:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:performance of the  borrower and based on that bank decides whether to renew the  facilities 
56:2673:127852:16:17:72:479:245:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:or not. The tools used for monitoring are portfolio review, profitability analysis etc.  
56:2674:127940:17:17:72:75:228:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
56:2675:127940:17:16:72:255:211:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:C4: Lack of Taking Proper Action: 
56:2676:127973:16:16:72:526:195:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Action  comes  after  loan  monitoring.  Monitoring  is  done  for  identifying  deviations  or 
56:2677:128069:16:17:72:526:179:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:exceptions.  If  there  is  any  exception  then  corrective  action  needs  to  be  taken.  If  corrective 
56:2678:128177:17:17:72:526:162:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:actions  are  taken  on  time  chance  of  default  loan  reduces.  When  customer  misses  one 
56:2679:128273:17:16:72:526:145:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:installment, concerned officer of the  bank  must visit the customer and understand where the 
56:2680:128367:16:17:72:445:129:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:problem lies. If proper action is taken, probability of loan default is reduced.  
56:2681:128448:17:16:72:75:112:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
56:2682:128448:16:17:72:75:96:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
56:2683:128448:17:0:72:75:79:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
57:2684:128450:0:16:72:217:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:D. Macroeconomic Factors: 
57:2685:128475:16:17:72:194:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:D1: Low GDP Growth: 
57:2686:128494:17:16:72:526:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:It  is  evident  that  companies  which  deal  in  consumer  products  are  directly  affected  by  the 
57:2687:128598:16:17:72:526:709:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:GDP  growth  of  the  entire  economy.  Regular  customers  and  defaulters  have  opined  that  this 
57:2688:128700:17:16:72:526:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:macro indicator influences the cash generation of a company and hence the repayment of the 
57:2689:128791:16:17:72:98:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:loan. 
57:2690:128796:17:17:72:75:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
57:2691:128796:17:16:72:195:642:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:D2: Increasing Crimes: 
57:2692:128818:16:17:72:526:626:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:It is revealed that the effect of the  increasing crimes  in the  business of the  companies. They 
57:2693:128917:17:17:72:488:609:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:think that forced subscription sometimes make the profitability of the company lower. 
57:2694:129002:17:16:72:257:592:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:D3: Hartals by the Political Parties: 
57:2695:129039:16:16:72:526:576:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Political instability of the country hampers the production and the distribution of the products 
57:2696:129136:16:17:72:526:560:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:in  a  smooth  way  and  the  the  political  turmoil  is  considered  one  of  other  causes  of  the  loan 
57:2697:129245:17:17:72:182:543:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:default in our country. 
57:2698:129268:17:16:72:75:526:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
57:2699:129268:16:17:72:333:510:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:D4: Frequent Policy Changed by the Government: 
57:2700:129314:17:16:72:526:493:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Government  policy  is  considered  as  the  minor  cause  of  the  loan  default  as  per  our  survey 
57:2701:129418:16:17:72:526:477:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:since it has a little impact on the local sales and distribution of the products of the companies. 
57:2702:129517:17:16:72:526:460:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Without these are other causes such as imperfect lending practice, lack of analysis of business 
57:2703:129613:16:17:72:526:444:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:risks,  lack  of  proper  valuation  of  security  or  mortgage  property,  undue  influence  by 
57:2704:129710:17:16:72:526:427:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:borrowers,  external  pressure,  loan  of  Govt.  organization,  Govt.  policy  for  disbursement  of 
57:2705:129812:16:18:72:202:411:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:credit, lack of legal action. 
57:2706:129841:18:16:72:75:393:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:  
57:2707:129841:16:16:72:359:377:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:6.2: Indicators and Remedies of Loan Default Problem: 
57:2708:129894:16:17:72:526:361:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Before  analyzing  the  remedies  of  loan  default  problems  we  will  discuss  the  indicators  of 
57:2709:129996:17:16:72:526:344:12:Times New Roman:12:g_d0_f9:default loan which would indicate financial trouble and serve as a “red flag” to the financial 
57:2710:130091:16:17:72:526:328:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:officer. There are many indicators of default loans but there is no set pattern of frequency of 
57:2711:130187:17:17:72:510:311:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:occurrences of events leading up to a point where a loan could be declared a problem loan. 
57:2712:130277:17:16:72:75:294:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:  
57:2713:130277:16:18:72:230:278:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:A. Indicators of Default Loan: 
57:2714:130307:18:17:90:319:260:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Delayed submission of financial statements 
57:2715:130350:17:17:90:486:243:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Slowness in the ability to arrange plants visits and deterioration in the rapport  
57:2716:130433:17:18:90:508:226:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Declining deposit balances and the occurrences of overdrafts and returned cheques 
57:2717:130515:18:17:90:402:208:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: An unusual rise in inventories and increase in trade payables 
57:2718:130577:17:17:90:526:191:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: An  increase  in  receivables,  this  may  indicate  a  lowering  in  the  qualities  of  the  firms 
57:2719:130679:17:16:90:526:174:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:products or services, a change in the terms of sale , or the sale to financially weak firms in 
57:2720:130774:16:18:90:273:158:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:an effort to increase sales and income 
57:2721:130812:18:17:90:516:140:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Expansion through merger or acquisition : merger with another firm or sale of assets 
57:2722:130897:17:18:90:251:123:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Irregular payment of the loan 
57:2723:130927:18:17:90:468:105:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Change in management or the resignation of key personnel, labor problem 
57:2724:130999:17:0:90:308:88:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: New financial arrangement or indebtness 
58:2725:131041:0:16:90:300:757:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Natural disasters such as flood, fire etc. 
58:2726:131084:16:14:72:75:741:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
58:2727:131084:14:16:72:239:727:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:B. Remedies of Default Loans:    
58:2728:131116:16:17:72:526:711:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Keeping  in  mind  the  above  indicators  we  can  proceed  on  to  find  out  some  remedies. 
58:2729:131212:17:17:72:526:694:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:According  to  Prof.  Muzaffer  Ahmad(1997)  the  way  out  of  the  current  crisis  of  bank  loan 
58:2730:131313:17:16:72:526:677:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:default  lies  in  evolution  and  entrenchment  of  responsive  and  participate  governance  from 
58:2731:131413:16:17:72:526:661:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:grass roots upwards which can be instrumental in  decartelizing the decision making process. 
58:2732:131506:17:16:72:526:644:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:In this visualized governance process the governments will take on itself the task of removing 
58:2733:131601:16:17:72:526:628:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:imperfections  due  to  invisibilities,  externalities,  imperfect  access  to  information,  knowledge 
58:2734:131705:17:16:72:526:611:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:and resources (Ahmad 1997). Bhattacharya (1998) highlights the crucial need of building up 
58:2735:131796:16:17:72:526:595:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:a strong  financial  infrastructure an adequate  legal  framework for enforcing  lenders' recourse 
58:2736:131895:17:16:72:525:578:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:on   borrowers,   effective   supervisory   and   regulatory   role   of   the   central   bank   through 
58:2737:132001:16:17:72:526:562:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:formulation    of    broad-based    prudential    guidelines,    commercial    autonomy    of    bank 
58:2738:132103:17:17:72:526:545:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:management, and institution of a readable  and transparent accounting base. He mentions the 
58:2739:132195:17:16:72:526:528:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:following reform Issues   such as autonomy of Bangladesh Bank should  be  strengthened and 
58:2740:132286:16:17:72:526:512:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the post of governor should  be  made  constitutional, role of  banking division of the Ministry 
58:2741:132383:17:16:72:526:495:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of  Finance should be reduced, the Scheduled banks should be put fully under the regulatory 
58:2742:132475:16:17:72:526:479:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:oversight of the Bangladesh Bank (corporate governance of the banks), members of political 
58:2743:132566:17:16:72:526:462:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:parties  and  defaulters  should  be  barred  from  the  boards  of  directors  of  banks,    state  owned 
58:2744:132673:16:17:72:526:446:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:enterprises  should  be  pursued  for  defaulter  loans,  loan  amnesty  and  loan  forgiveness 
58:2745:132769:17:17:72:526:429:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:undermines  financial  discipline,    PCBs  should  not  be  bailed  out  through  re-capitalization, 
58:2746:132871:17:16:72:526:412:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:which may encourage moral hazard, International Standard based audit of the loan portfolio, 
58:2747:132963:16:17:72:526:396:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:assets, liabilities and capital adequacy should be introduced for a full and proper disclosure of 
58:2748:133061:17:16:72:526:379:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the financial situation of the banks, elimination of remaining restrains on interest fixation by 
58:2749:133158:16:17:72:526:363:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the  banks  should  be  expedited,  alternatives  for  industrial  finance  should  be  explored  ( 
58:2750:133258:17:16:72:526:346:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:NBFLs),  wider  use  of  on-leading  mechanisms  through  the  Grameen  Bank  and  the  NGOs 
58:2751:133351:16:17:72:526:330:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(MFIs) should be a way-out for small for and micro-credit. diversification of product base of 
58:2752:133445:17:17:72:526:313:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:banks  :  Venture  capital,  factoring,  asset  securitization,  leasing,  and  consumer  product 
58:2753:133543:17:16:72:526:296:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:financing,  issuance  linked  deposit  schemes,  mutual  funds,  card  business,  certificates  of 
58:2754:133642:16:17:72:526:280:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:deposit, etc. integrated computerized and upgradation of professional skills of officials should 
58:2755:133739:17:16:72:526:263:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:be taken up on a priority basis, delinking of pay scales of bankers from the national pay scale 
58:2756:133835:16:17:72:525:247:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:should  be  expedited  and  Strategic  Business  Plans  to  reduce  excess  manpower  should  be 
58:2757:133932:17:16:72:526:230:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:undertaken,    privatization  of  banks  on  ideological  grounds  should  be  stopped.  It  must  be 
58:2758:134034:16:17:72:213:214:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:based on empirical grounds.  
58:2759:134062:17:14:72:75:197:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
58:2760:134062:14:16:72:526:183:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:The agenda outlined above contain the key elements of a comprehensive action plan, which, 
58:2761:134152:16:17:72:526:167:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:if  pursued  in  right  earnest,  can  effectively  arrest  the  deterioration  of  the  trend  of  mounting 
58:2762:134261:17:16:72:526:150:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:bank loan default, we believe. The proposed amendments of existing laws and the enactment 
58:2763:134351:16:17:72:365:134:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of new laws will help in achieving the following objectives:  
58:2764:134412:17:17:72:75:117:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
58:2765:134412:17:17:94:526:100:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The  amendments  will  increase  Bangladesh  Bank's  autonomy  and  power  to  regulate 
58:2766:134501:17:0:94:394:83:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:and supervise (both on-site and off-site) the financial system.  
59:2767:134567:0:16:94:526:757:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The amendments should  be designed to severely restrict  insider  lending plaguing the 
59:2768:134655:16:18:94:233:741:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:private commercial banks.    
59:2769:134683:18:16:94:526:723:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The  amendments  should  aim  at  providing  exemplary  punishments  to  people  issuing 
59:2770:134773:16:18:94:410:707:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:had cheques and banks involved in corruption and malpractice's.  
59:2771:134837:18:17:94:413:689:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: They should be designed to improve the governance of NCBs.  
59:2772:134897:17:17:94:367:672:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: They should improve the deposit insurance schemes.  
59:2773:134949:17:17:94:526:655:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The  new  laws will provide effective  mechanism to pursue the willful defaulters. The 
59:2774:135037:17:16:94:525:638:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:proposed tribunal should be entrusted to deal with cases of the top 500 defaulters only to 
59:2775:135128:16:17:94:372:622:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:speed up the disposal of the recovery cases significantly.  
59:2776:135187:17:17:72:75:605:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
59:2777:135187:17:16:72:275:588:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:6.3: Recommendations of World Bank: 
59:2778:135222:16:17:72:388:572:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:6.3.1 The officer of the Ombudsman for the Financial Sector: 
59:2779:135281:17:16:72:526:555:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:The  proposed  office  of  ombudsman  for  the  financial  sector  will  be  responsible  only  to  the 
59:2780:135385:16:17:72:526:539:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Board  of  Director  of  Bangladesh  Bank.  The  ombudsman  will  be  helped  by a  network  of 
59:2781:135481:17:16:72:526:522:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:ethics  in each  bank.  Who will  be responsible only to the respective  Boars of Directors? The 
59:2782:135578:16:17:72:526:506:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:office of ombudsman will deal with complaints of malpractices and corruption in the banking 
59:2783:135670:17:17:72:526:489:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:sector  independently,  and  will  recommend  appropriate  punishments  for  the  investigated 
59:2784:135765:17:16:72:106:472:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:cases.  
59:2785:135772:16:17:72:75:456:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
59:2786:135772:17:17:72:325:439:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:6.3.2 De-politicization of Governance of Banks: 
59:2787:135818:17:17:94:526:422:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: A management selection committee should be formed to recommend appointments of 
59:2788:135898:17:17:94:301:405:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:members of the boards of different banks.  
59:2789:135940:17:17:94:526:388:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: International  auditing  and  accounting  standards  should  be  uniformly  followed  in  all 
59:2790:136035:17:17:94:493:371:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the banks to bring transparency and comparability of accounts of different banks.   
59:2791:136118:17:18:94:352:354:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Financial control systems should be standardized.  
59:2792:136169:18:16:94:526:336:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Trade unions should  be delinked  from direct political  affiliations, and the  number of 
59:2793:136260:16:18:94:356:320:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:trade unions should be limited to three for each bank.  
59:2794:136315:18:17:94:461:302:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The post of Governor of Bangladesh Bank should be made constitutional 
59:2795:136385:17:16:94:526:285:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The  banking  division  of  the  Ministry  of  Finance  should  be  entrusted  the  role  of 
59:2796:136479:16:18:94:532:269:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:supervising the NCBs and the specialized banks remaining under government ownership.   
59:2797:136565:18:16:94:450:251:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: The autonomy of Bangladesh Bank should get the priority it deserves.  
59:2798:136635:16:17:72:75:235:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
59:2799:136635:17:17:72:215:218:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:6.3.3 Enforcement of Laws: 
59:2800:136661:17:16:72:526:201:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:The legal system allows defaulters to delay lenders recourse process indefinitely, making the 
59:2801:136755:16:17:72:525:185:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:enforcement process a virtual mockery. Therefore, the issue of establishing a specialized debt 
59:2802:136850:17:16:72:446:168:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:collection agency for pursuing the top 500 defaulters needs special attention.  
59:2803:136929:16:17:72:75:152:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
59:2804:136929:17:17:72:179:135:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:6.4 Other Remedies: 
59:2805:136948:17:17:94:526:118:12:g_d0_f11:12:g_d0_f9: Banking  profitability  in  the  long  run  depends  on  a  bank‟s  ability  to  collect  and 
59:2806:137043:17:0:94:526:101:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:analyze  information  and  to  put  optimal  conditions  to  its  loan  supply.  To  develop  this 
60:2807:137144:0:16:94:525:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:ability,  financial  institutions  must  be  in  a  condition  of  sound  market  competition  and 
60:2808:137243:16:18:94:258:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:appropriate prudential regulation. 
60:2809:137277:18:16:94:526:724:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Considering credit as a scarce resources and source of economic and political power, 
60:2810:137363:16:17:94:525:708:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:all  the  societies  around  the  world  are  careful  about  its  distribution  and  use.  In  order  to 
60:2811:137469:17:16:94:525:691:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:best utilize credit an attempt should be made in order to avoid concentration of loans into 
60:2812:137561:16:18:94:149:675:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:few hands. 
60:2813:137571:18:16:94:526:657:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Strengthening   the   security   market   will have   a   positive   impact   on   the   overall 
60:2814:137668:16:17:94:525:641:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:development  of  the  banking  sector  by  increasing  the  competitiveness  in  the  financial 
60:2815:137764:17:16:94:525:624:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:sector. In a developed capital market the range of portfolio selection is wider and people 
60:2816:137855:16:17:94:526:608:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:can  compare  the  security  of  their  investment  among  the  banks  and  the  security  market. 
60:2817:137954:17:17:94:498:591:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:As a result banks remain under some pressure to improve their financial soundness. 
60:2818:138036:17:17:94:526:574:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Bangladesh has a bright prospect in the sectors of small and medium scale enterprises. 
60:2819:138124:17:17:94:525:557:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Poorer  sections  of  the  society  have  innate  entrepreneurial  ability  of  undertaking  some 
60:2820:138222:17:16:94:525:540:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:small  profitable  projects.  Successful  operation  of  some  NGOs  (Grameen  Bank  and 
60:2821:138311:16:17:94:525:524:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:BRAC  are  few  of  them)  provides  evidences  that  the  poor  people  can  be  bankable  even 
60:2822:138408:17:17:94:187:507:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:without collateral.  
60:2823:138428:17:17:94:526:490:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Bangladesh  may  look  for  and utilize  a  number  of  merger  and  acquisition  cases 
60:2824:138516:17:16:94:525:473:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:especially among the larger banks if any for the better information sharing, management, 
60:2825:138605:16:17:94:249:457:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:and diversification of activities. 
60:2826:138639:17:16:94:97:440:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
60:2827:138639:16:17:72:526:424:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:In    the  Bangladesh  banking  sector,  the  main  conflict  is  that  the  loss  due  to  inefficiency  of 
60:2828:138748:17:16:72:526:407:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:collection  of  bad  loans  for  whatever  reasons,  where  the  shareholders  are  definitely  not 
60:2829:138848:16:17:72:526:391:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:responsible, are adjusted by  making provisions out of profit and then utilizing this provision 
60:2830:138944:17:17:72:526:374:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:to write off bad loans, the collection of which is uncertain. It may not be justified because the 
60:2831:139041:17:16:72:526:357:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:amount  and  payment  sys  tem  is  not  linked  to  performance,  especially  in  case  of  less  than 
60:2832:139145:16:17:72:526:341:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:average performance. To minimize this conflict, loan classification should be stopped, that is, 
60:2833:139241:17:16:72:525:324:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:regular repayment should be ensured. This will reduce the provision for the loan loss amount, 
60:2834:139335:16:17:72:526:308:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:which  in  turn  will  result  in  more  tax  payment  and  more  after tax  profit  of  the  organization, 
60:2835:139443:17:16:72:526:291:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:which  is  the  precondition  for  maximization  of  shareholders‟  wealth.  Provision  in  other 
60:2836:139541:16:17:72:525:275:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:business is an estimation based on the past experience of the uncollectible amounts. If banks 
60:2837:139635:17:17:72:526:258:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:can  stop  classification,  then  1  percent  of  unclassified  loans  will  suffice  or  in  the  future  this 
60:2838:139747:17:16:72:526:241:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:percentage may also reduced: “Prevention is better than cure. This should be the watchword 
60:2839:139838:16:17:72:526:225:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:for  monitoring  and  supervising  loan  accounts  of  bank.  Making  classification  and  pursuing 
60:2840:139938:17:16:72:526:208:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:borrowers  to  regularize  the  accounts  rarely  meet  success.  The  cost  of  such  exercise  is  also 
60:2841:140044:16:17:72:526:192:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:heavy.  So,  the  bank  should   evolve  appropriate  systems  to  detect  deficiencies   in  the 
60:2842:140142:17:16:72:526:175:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:management  of  credit  operations  well  before  it  calls  for  classification.  In  this  regard  an 
60:2843:140246:16:17:72:526:159:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:effective on-site and off-site supervision system should be in place both in the schedule banks 
60:2844:140342:17:16:72:255:142:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:and central banks (Alam and Jahan).” 
60:2845:140378:16:17:72:75:126:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:

62:2921:141302:0:14:242:325:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Chapter- Seven 
62:2922:141315:14:14:282:285:744:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
62:2923:141315:14:14:128:439:730:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Summary of Findings, Challenges and Concluding Remarks 
62:2924:141369:14:14:297:300:716:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
62:2925:141369:14:8:72:289:702:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:7.1 Summary of Findings and Challenges: 
62:2926:141408:8:12:72:74:694:6:Times New Roman:6:Times New Roman: 
62:2927:141408:12:17:72:526:682:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:The  foregoing  discussion  regarding  NPLs  in  Bangladesh  reveals  that  the  banking  sector  of 
62:2928:141509:17:17:72:526:665:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Bangladesh  is  yet  to  get  out  of  its  NPL  mess,  although  substantial  improvement  has  been 
62:2929:141611:17:16:72:526:648:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:noticed recently. In terms of adoption of the international loan classification and provisioning 
62:2930:141708:16:17:72:526:632:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:system, Bangladesh follows the international standard (table 2) to a great extent, but lags far 
62:2931:141804:17:16:72:526:615:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:behind  with  regard  to  the  management  of  NPLs.  At  present  (2011),  the  banking  system  of 
62:2932:141905:16:17:72:525:599:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Bangladesh exhibits a very high proportion of NPLs (6.59%) when compared to India and Sri 
62:2933:141995:17:16:72:526:582:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:Lanka is lower. The most dissatisfactory performance is seen in the management of “bad 
62:2934:142082:16:17:72:526:566:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:loans” which consistently account for more than 80% of total NPLs (table 5). This situation 
62:2935:142174:17:17:72:525:549:12:Times New Roman:12:g_d0_f9:clearly demonstrates the inefficacy of the banking system to tackle the “flow problem of bad 
62:2936:142267:17:16:72:526:532:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:loans”. Therefore, the first challenge  facing the banking sector of Bangladesh  is  how to 
62:2937:142359:16:17:72:473:516:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:constitute sufficient measures to address the flow problem of bad loans effectively. 
62:2938:142443:17:16:72:75:499:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
62:2939:142443:16:17:72:526:483:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:It  is  observed  that  among  the  different  clusters  of  banks  in  Bangladesh,  SCBs  and  DFIs 
62:2940:142544:17:16:72:526:466:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:continue to have an alarming amount of NPLs is 14.1% and 21.8% respectively in 2011 since 
62:2941:142634:16:17:72:526:450:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the  adoption  of  prudential  norms  in  1990.    Although  it  is  not  clear  which  sectors  contain 
62:2942:142739:17:16:72:526:433:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:major  NPLs,  available  data  indicates  that  the  highest  ratio  of  NPLs  are  in  the  category  of 
62:2943:142845:16:17:72:526:417:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:loans  of  both  SCBs  and  DFIs  are14.1%  and  21.8%  respectively,  followed  by  term  loans 
62:2944:142942:17:17:72:526:400:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:having a maturity of more than 20 years in the case of DFIs (Table 6).  The NPL ratio of term 
62:2945:143036:17:16:72:526:383:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:loans given  by SCBs  is also observed to be very  high.  Another  important observation  is the 
62:2946:143133:16:17:72:526:367:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:gradual reduction of capital in SCBs due to maintenance of poor loan loss provisions against 
62:2947:143226:17:16:72:526:350:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:default loans (table 7). These aspects clearly call for ending the operation of SCBs and DFIs. 
62:2948:143321:16:17:72:526:334:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:However, it needs to be mentioned here that the stock markets of Bangladesh are not efficient 
62:2949:143415:17:16:72:526:317:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:enough to channel funds for industrial growth, and thus SCBs as well as DFIs play a vital role 
62:2950:143510:16:17:72:525:301:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:in  meeting the  overall  industrial  credit  needs  of  the  country.  Hence,  the  second  challenge 
62:2951:143613:17:17:72:526:284:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:before the  banking  system  is to decide whether to stop operations of the SCBs and DFIs, to 
62:2952:143707:17:16:72:450:267:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:privatize them, or to reorient them through financial engineering in full phase. 
62:2953:143787:16:17:72:75:251:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
62:2954:143787:17:16:72:526:234:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:The study   reveals   the   dissatisfactory   performance   of   the   courts   (Money   loan   Court, 
62:2955:143889:16:17:72:526:218:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Bankruptcy Court and PDR Court) in terms of rate of settlement of NPL disputes as well  as 
62:2956:143980:17:16:72:526:201:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:rate of recovery of loans over the years in review (tables 9&10). The main problem related to 
62:2957:144074:16:17:72:526:185:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:very  low  recovery  lies  in  the  very  slow  execution  of  the  decrees.  The  Financial  Sector 
62:2958:144175:17:17:72:526:168:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Reform  Project  (FSRP)  argues  that  the  huge  loan  delinquency  of  the  Bangladesh  banking 
62:2959:144273:17:16:72:526:151:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:system  reflects,  among  other  things,  the  weakness  of  the  legal  infrastructure,  which  cannot 
62:2960:144377:16:17:72:526:135:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:ensure lenders‟ recourse on borrowers. The inefficacy on the part of the legal system also 
62:2961:144468:17:16:72:526:118:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:sometimes  encourages  borrowers  to  refrain  from  paying  legitimate  dues  to  the  banks.  The 
62:2962:144568:16:17:72:526:102:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Center  for  Policy  Dialogue  (CPD)  Task  Force  Report  (2001)  also  indicates  that  the  main 
62:2963:144668:17:0:72:526:85:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:hindrance  at  this  moment  in  Bangladesh  is  the  existing  legal  framework  and  its  lengthy 
63:2964:144770:0:16:72:526:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:procedures.  However,  if  the  delay  in  the  settlement  process  arises  due  to  the  shortage  of 
63:2965:144874:16:17:72:526:742:12:g_d0_f9:12:Times New Roman:judges, then separate posts like “Bank Magistrates” can be created to settle NPL issues. It is 
63:2966:144969:17:16:72:526:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:to be kept in mind, however, that without having the proper cooperation and sincerity of the 
63:2967:145062:16:17:72:526:709:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:concerned  individuals,  the  law  itself  can  by  no  means  expedite  the  process.  Thus,  the  third 
63:2968:145168:17:16:72:526:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:challenge before the banking sector is how to ensure cooperation, sincerity and accountability 
63:2969:145262:16:17:72:526:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of  the  involved  parties  like  plaintiff,  defendants,  lawyers  and  judges,  in  order  to  make  the 
63:2970:145369:17:17:72:259:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:settlement process vibrant and speedy. 
63:2971:145407:17:16:72:75:642:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
63:2972:145407:16:17:72:526:626:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Concerning  recovery  strategies  by  artha-rin  adatal,  it  is  observed  that  Bangladesh  has 
63:2973:145505:17:16:72:526:609:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:concentrated  mainly  on  legal  measures  to  address  the  NPL  issue  (table  8).  Unfortunately, 
63:2974:145606:16:17:72:526:593:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:these  legal  measures  have  been  found  to  be  very  time  consuming,  resource  draining  and 
63:2975:145705:17:16:72:529:576:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:ineffective,  and  have  ultimately  resulted  in  poor recovery  performance  (table  9  &  10).  
63:2976:145804:16:17:72:526:560:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Interestingly,  despite  being  aware  of  this  fact, the  banking  system  of  Bangladesh  has  barely 
63:2977:145909:17:17:72:525:543:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:begun  to  adopt  non-legal  measures  such  as  out of  court  settlements,  compromise  settlement 
63:2978:146010:17:16:72:526:526:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:schemes,  formation  of  loan  workout departments  etc.  as  operate  in  India  for  the  effective 
63:2979:146112:16:17:72:526:510:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:recovery  of  NPLs.  Therefore,  the  fourth  challenge  confronting  the  banking  sector  is  how  to 
63:2980:146216:17:16:72:526:493:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:constitute a concrete NPL management strategy equipped with both preventive and resolution 
63:2981:146307:16:17:72:122:477:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:measures. 
63:2982:146316:17:16:72:75:460:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
63:2983:146316:16:17:72:525:444:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:In a bank-centered financial system, it is very crucial to determine whether the defaulter is a 
63:2984:146412:17:16:72:526:427:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:willful one or a genuine one. In the case of the  former,  if timely  and adequate  measures  are 
63:2985:146510:16:17:72:526:411:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:not  taken  and  problems  are  left  unresolved,  the  willful  defaulters  can  have a  psychological 
63:2986:146613:17:17:72:526:394:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:impact on good borrowers, acting as a catalyst to financial degradation. In fact, in developing 
63:2987:146709:17:16:72:526:377:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:countries  like  Bangladesh,  a  large  number  of  willful  defaulters  operate  in  the  financial 
63:2988:146810:16:17:72:526:361:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:market,  trying  to  degrade  the  credit  environment  either  by  window-dressing  their  financial 
63:2989:146912:17:16:72:526:344:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:health  or  by  influencing  the  bank  management  through  vested  groups,  or  both.  In  many 
63:2990:147010:16:17:72:526:328:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:reports (BRC, SAPRI, CPD), serious concerns have been shown about the presence of willful 
63:2991:147100:17:16:72:526:311:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:defaulters in Bangladesh and it has been suggested that loan facilities should not be offered to 
63:2992:147197:16:17:72:526:295:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:this  group.  Nevertheless,  in  reality,  the  banking  system  has  not  yet  come  up  with  any 
63:2993:147297:17:17:72:526:278:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:effective strategies to identify the habitual defaulters and to take action against them. In this 
63:2994:147395:17:16:72:525:261:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:regard,  a  prominent challenge  before  the  banking  sector  could  be  seen  as  how  to  develop 
63:2995:147495:16:17:72:497:245:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:specific tools and techniques to distinguish the willful defaulters from the genuine ones. 
63:2996:147585:17:16:72:75:228:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
63:2997:147585:16:17:72:526:212:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Almost  a  decade  ago,  the  banking  system  of  Bangladesh  adopted  a  lending  risk  analysis 
63:2998:147684:17:16:72:526:195:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:(LRA) device – a prescribed manual given by FSRP for analyzing loans of Tk. 10 million and 
63:2999:147774:16:17:72:525:179:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:above – with the objective of gauging the intensity of risk associated with large loans and to 
63:3000:147868:17:17:72:526:162:12:Times New Roman:12:g_d0_f9:choose loan proposals with low risk exposures. LRA has now been superseded by the “credit 
63:3001:147958:17:16:72:526:145:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:risk grading system” for better identification and management of borrower‟s risk. However, 
63:3002:148049:16:17:72:526:129:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the  application  of  this  sophisticated  technique  (CRG)  as  a  credit  screening  and  monitoring 
63:3003:148152:17:16:72:526:112:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:tool  largely  depends  on  sufficient  business  data  and  know-how  of  the  concerned  credit 
63:3004:148250:16:17:72:526:96:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:officials.  Surprisingly,  these  are  seen  to  be  very  poor  in  the  credit  environment  of  this 
63:3005:148354:17:0:72:526:79:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:country.  Thus,  the  appropriate  authorities  should  pay  proper  heed  to  redressing  these 
64:3006:148453:0:16:72:526:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:problems  to  ensure  meaningful  application  of  the  CRG  device  in  the  credit  environment  of 
64:3007:148555:16:17:72:136:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Bangladesh.  
64:3008:148567:17:16:72:75:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
64:3009:148567:16:17:72:526:709:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:After the financial crisis of 1997, the East Asian countries (China, Malaysia, Singapore, and 
64:3010:148661:17:16:72:526:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Indonesia) realized that asset  management companies can play a  vital role  in addressing the 
64:3011:148756:16:17:72:526:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:bad  loan  problem  and  can ensure  robust  financial  discipline.  Recently,  India  has  set  up  an 
64:3012:148859:17:17:72:526:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:asset  management company as a trust to reorganize their  bad  loans. India  has also  instituted 
64:3013:148957:17:16:72:526:642:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f9:“factoring devices” and “asset securitisation techniques” to remove NPLs from the balance 
64:3014:149047:16:17:72:525:626:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:sheet of  a  bank.  In  Bangladesh,  however,  no  initiative  has  been  taken  so  far  towards  the 
64:3015:149150:17:16:72:526:609:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:formation of an asset management company which could undertake activities relating to asset 
64:3016:149242:16:17:72:526:593:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:reconstruction and develop markets for distressed assets. Factoring devices and securitisation 
64:3017:149337:17:16:72:526:576:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:techniques are hardly ever employed for the removal of NPLs in Bangladesh. Therefore, the 
64:3018:149427:16:17:72:526:560:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:next challenge  before the  banking  sector is  how to set up an asset  management company or 
64:3019:149521:17:17:72:525:543:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:institute  factoring  services  and  asset  securitisation  techniques  that  would  address  NPLs 
64:3020:149620:17:16:72:293:526:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:effectively without generating moral hazards. 
64:3021:149664:16:17:72:75:510:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
64:3022:149664:17:16:72:526:493:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:This study reveals that the highest loan defaults are in the category of micro and agricultural 
64:3023:149760:16:17:72:526:477:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:credits,  followed  by  term  loans  /  large  loans  having  maturity  of  20  years  and  more  than 20 
64:3024:149865:17:16:72:526:460:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:years (table 5). To resolve this  issue, the  loan  syndication technique  might be considered  as 
64:3025:149964:16:17:72:526:444:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:an   effective   financial   tool.   However,   proper   application   of   this   technique   requires 
64:3026:150068:17:16:72:526:427:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:cooperation, sincerity and transparency among banks, practices which are seen to be absent in 
64:3027:150162:16:17:72:526:411:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the  country  at  present.  Moreover,  bankers  have  been  observed  to  engage  in  unhealthy 
64:3028:150258:17:17:72:526:394:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:competition  in the  market.  Therefore, another  issue  is  how to exercise syndicated  financing 
64:3029:150357:17:16:72:434:377:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:technique minimizing unhealthy competition among banks in Bangladesh.  
64:3030:150427:16:17:72:75:361:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
64:3031:150427:17:16:72:526:344:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Finally,  maintenance  of  an  ethical  standard  in  the  banking  profession  from  all  concerns  can 
64:3032:150532:16:17:72:526:328:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:be  viewed  as  an  important  means  for  making  the  credit  environment  credible  and  vibrant. 
64:3033:150633:17:16:72:526:311:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Ethics  contributes  great  deals  to  fair  practices  of  lending  when  law  itself  becomes  impotent 
64:3034:150739:16:17:72:526:295:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:due to invisible contingencies. Hence, the importance of ethics in financial institutions should 
64:3035:150836:17:17:72:164:278:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:not be overlooked. 
64:3036:150854:17:16:72:75:261:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
64:3037:150854:16:9:72:206:245:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:7.2 Concluding Remarks: 
64:3038:150877:9:13:72:73:236:4:Times New Roman:4:Times New Roman: 
64:3039:150877:13:17:72:527:223:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:More than 20 years have passed since the adoption of prudential norms in the banking system 
64:3040:150968:17:16:72:526:206:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:of Bangladesh in 1990. Unfortunately, the banking system is still burdened with an alarming 
64:3041:151060:16:17:72:529:190:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:amount  of  NPLs  and  lags  far  behind  the  neighboring  countries  of  India  and  Sri  Lanka.  
64:3042:151160:17:16:72:526:173:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Although   Bangladesh   has   to   a   large   degree   adopted   international   standards   of   loan 
64:3043:151264:16:17:72:526:157:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:classification and provisioning, the  management of  NPLs  is  found  ineffective, as the  system 
64:3044:151362:17:17:72:526:140:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:has  failed  to  arrest  fresh  NPLs  significantly.  It  needs  to  be  mentioned  that  management  of 
64:3045:151467:17:16:72:526:123:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:NPLs must be multi-pronged, with different strategies pursued at the different stages through 
64:3046:151560:16:17:72:526:107:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:which a credit facility passes. Measures should be in place for both prevention and resolution. 
64:3047:151656:17:0:72:526:90:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:With  regard  to  preventive  measures,  emphasis  needs  to  be  placed  on  credit  screening,  loan 
65:3048:151761:0:16:72:525:758:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:surveillance  and  loan  review  functionaries  both  at  individual  bank  levels  and  in  the  central 
65:3049:151867:16:17:72:526:742:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:bank  of  the  country.  Resolution  measures  must  be  accompanied  by  legal  measures,  i.e. 
65:3050:151964:17:16:72:526:725:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:improving the efficiency of the legal and the judicial system and developing other out of the 
65:3051:152058:16:17:72:526:709:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:court   settlement   measures   like   compromise   settlement   schemes,   incentive   packaging, 
65:3052:152157:17:16:72:526:692:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:formation  of  asset  management  companies,  factoring,  and  asset  securitisation  and  so  on. 
65:3053:152256:16:17:72:526:676:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:Unfortunately,  Bangladesh  is  found  to  be  very  weak  from  the  above  point  of  view,  and 
65:3054:152355:17:17:72:526:659:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:strictly  speaking,  it has  mainly  concentrated  on  a  few  legal  measures  that  have  also  been 
65:3055:152457:17:16:72:526:642:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:found to be ineffective. Therefore, this study has highlighted some challenges, shown below, 
65:3056:152550:16:17:72:526:626:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:for improving the debt recovery environment and solving the NPL problems of the country as 
65:3057:152641:17:16:72:98:609:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:well. 
65:3058:152646:16:18:72:75:593:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman: 
65:3059:152646:18:17:94:518:575:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To institute sufficient measures to address the flow problem of bad loans effectively. 
65:3060:152733:17:17:94:526:558:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To decide whether to stop operations of the SCBs and DFIs, to privatize them, or to 
65:3061:152818:17:17:94:309:541:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:reorient them through financial engineering. 
65:3062:152862:17:17:94:526:524:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To  ensure  cooperation,  sincerity  and accountability  of  involved  parties  such  as 
65:3063:152951:17:16:94:525:507:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:plaintiffs,  defendants,  lawyers  and  judges  to  make  the  settlement  process  vibrant  and 
65:3064:153048:16:18:94:133:491:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:speedy. 
65:3065:153055:18:16:94:526:473:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To  institute  immediately  a  concrete  NPL  management  strategy  equipped  with  both 
65:3066:153145:16:18:94:270:457:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:preventive and resolution measures. 
65:3067:153180:18:16:94:526:439:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To develop specific tools and techniques to distinguish the willful defaulters from the 
65:3068:153269:16:18:94:163:423:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:genuine ones. 
65:3069:153282:18:16:94:526:405:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To pay proper attention to addressing problems relating to meaningful  application of 
65:3070:153369:16:18:94:376:389:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:the CRG device in the credit environment of Bangladesh.  
65:3071:153425:18:16:94:526:371:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman:   To establish an asset management company or to institute factoring services as 
65:3072:153507:16:17:94:526:355:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:well   as  asset  securitisation  technique  so  as  to  address  NPLs  effectively without 
65:3073:153598:17:17:94:221:338:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:generating moral hazards. 
65:3074:153623:17:17:94:526:321:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To exercise syndicated financing technique for large loans and to minimize unhealthy 
65:3075:153709:17:17:94:295:304:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:competition among banks in Bangladesh. 
65:3076:153747:17:17:94:526:287:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: To strengthen the supervisory and  monitoring  functions of Bangladesh Bank so as to 
65:3077:153833:17:17:94:307:270:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:discipline banks that engage in malpractice. 
65:3078:153877:17:17:94:526:253:12:g_d0_f11:12:Times New Roman: Finally,  to  place  emphasis  on  ethical  standards  in  the  banking  profession  from  all 
65:3079:153973:17:16:94:404:236:12:Times New Roman:12:Times New Roman:corners to make the credit environment trustworthy and vibrant.
